  Code Structure

  # simulation/state.py

  from dataclasses import dataclass
  from typing import Optional
  import torch

  @dataclass
  class SimulationState:
      """
      Pure data container - NO methods that modify state.
      All tensors on same device.
      """

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # IONIC STATE
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      states: torch.Tensor          # [n_nodes, n_states] - V, gates, 
  concentrations

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # TIME
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      t: torch.Tensor               # Scalar - current simulation time

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # SPATIAL (set once at init)
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      nodes: torch.Tensor           # [n_nodes, 2] - x, y coordinates
      elements: torch.Tensor        # [n_elem, 3] - triangle vertex indices

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # FEM MATRICES (set once at init)
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      M: torch.Tensor               # Sparse [n, n] - mass matrix
      K: torch.Tensor               # Sparse [n, n] - stiffness matrix
      A: Optional[torch.Tensor]     # Sparse [n, n] - LHS matrix (precomputed)
      B: Optional[torch.Tensor]     # Sparse [n, n] - RHS matrix (precomputed)

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # STIMULUS (precomputed)
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      stim_masks: torch.Tensor      # [n_stim, n_nodes] - bool masks
      stim_times: torch.Tensor      # [n_stim, 2] - start, end times
      stim_amps: torch.Tensor       # [n_stim] - amplitudes

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # SOLVER WORKSPACE (pre-allocated)
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      pcg_r: torch.Tensor           # [n_nodes] - residual
      pcg_p: torch.Tensor           # [n_nodes] - search direction
      pcg_Ap: torch.Tensor          # [n_nodes] - A @ p
      pcg_x: torch.Tensor           # [n_nodes] - solution (warm start)

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # OUTPUT
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      output_buffer: torch.Tensor   # [buffer_size, n_nodes] - saved V
      buffer_idx: int               # Current position in buffer

      @property
      def n_nodes(self) -> int:
          return self.states.shape[0]

      @property
      def n_states(self) -> int:
          return self.states.shape[1]

      @property
      def device(self) -> torch.device:
          return self.states.device


  def create_state(mesh, ionic_model, config, device) -> SimulationState:
      """Factory function to initialize all state tensors."""
      n = mesh.n_nodes
      n_st = ionic_model.n_states

      return SimulationState(
          states=ionic_model.get_initial_state(n).to(device),
          t=torch.tensor(0.0, device=device),
          nodes=mesh.nodes.to(device),
          elements=mesh.elements.to(device),
          M=mesh.M.to(device),
          K=mesh.K.to(device),
          A=None,  # Set later by time stepper
          B=None,
          stim_masks=torch.zeros(0, n, dtype=torch.bool, device=device),
          stim_times=torch.zeros(0, 2, device=device),
          stim_amps=torch.zeros(0, device=device),
          pcg_r=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
          pcg_p=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
          pcg_Ap=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
          pcg_x=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
          output_buffer=torch.zeros(config.buffer_size, n, device=device),
          buffer_idx=0,
      )

  ---
  2. monodomain.py - The Orchestrator

  Purpose

  Coordinates the simulation steps. Calls ionic, diffusion, stimulus in order.

  ELI5

  The conductor of an orchestra - doesn't play instruments, just tells everyone
  when to play.

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”җ
  в”Ӯ                            monodomain.py
   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                          "The Conductor"
   в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”ҳ

  WHAT IT DOES:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ                         MonodomainSimulation                         в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   OWNS:                           COORDINATES:                       в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў state (SimulationState)       вҖў ionic_model.step()              в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў ionic_model                   вҖў time_stepper.step()             в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў time_stepper                  вҖў stimulus application            в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў config                        вҖў output saving                   в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                      в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   PROVIDES:                                                          в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў step(dt)        - One timestep                                  в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў run(t_end)      - Full simulation                               в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў add_stimulus()  - Add pacing protocol                           в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   вҖў get_results()   - Retrieve outputs                              в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
                                      в”Ӯ
                                      в”Ӯ Calls in sequence:
                                      в–ј
           в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
           в”Ӯ                                                          в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ   1. stimulus.apply(state, t)                           в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в–ј                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ   2. ionic_model.step(state.states, dt, Istim)          в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в–ј                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ   3. time_stepper.step(state, dt)  в”Җв”Җв–ә calls linear.py  в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в–ј                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ   4. save_output_if_needed(state)                       в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в”Ӯ                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ          в–ј                                               в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ   5. state.t += dt                                      в”Ӯ
           в”Ӯ                                                          в”Ӯ
           в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  WHAT IT DOES NOT DO:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  вң— Matrix math (delegated to time_stepper)
  вң— Ion channel kinetics (delegated to ionic_model)
  вң— Linear system solving (delegated to linear solver)
  вң— Device management (delegated to backend)

  Code Structure

  # simulation/monodomain.py

  from typing import Optional, Callable, List, Tuple
  import torch

  from .state import SimulationState, create_state
  from .stimulus import StimulusProtocol
  from ..solver.time_stepping import CrankNicolsonStepper
  from ..ionic.base import IonicModel

  @dataclass
  class SimulationConfig:
      """Configuration - separate from state."""
      dt: float = 0.02                # Time step (ms)
      D: float = 0.001                # Diffusion coefficient (cmВІ/ms)
      chi: float = 1400.0             # Surface-to-volume ratio (cmвҒ»В№)
      Cm: float = 1.0                 # Membrane capacitance (ВөF/cmВІ)
      save_interval: float = 1.0     # Save every N ms
      buffer_size: int = 1000         # Output buffer size
      pcg_tol: float = 1e-8
      pcg_max_iter: int = 50


  class MonodomainSimulation:
      """
      Orchestrates the monodomain simulation.
      
      Responsibilities:
      - Initialize state and components
      - Coordinate step execution order
      - Manage stimulus protocol
      - Handle output collection
      
      NOT responsible for:
      - Actual computation (delegated)
      - Device management (uses backend)
      """

      def __init__(
          self,
          mesh,
          ionic_model: IonicModel,
          config: SimulationConfig,
          backend
      ):
          self.config = config
          self.backend = backend
          self.ionic_model = ionic_model

          # Initialize state container
          self.state = create_state(
              mesh=mesh,
              ionic_model=ionic_model,
              config=config,
              device=backend.device
          )

          # Initialize time stepper (owns diffusion logic)
          self.time_stepper = CrankNicolsonStepper(
              M=self.state.M,
              K=self.state.K,
              dt=config.dt,
              theta=0.5,
              pcg_tol=config.pcg_tol,
              pcg_max_iter=config.pcg_max_iter
          )

          # Precompute LHS/RHS matrices
          self.state.A = self.time_stepper.A
          self.state.B = self.time_stepper.B

          # Stimulus protocol
          self.stimulus = StimulusProtocol(device=backend.device)

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # PUBLIC API
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def add_stimulus(self, region, start: float, duration: float, amplitude: 
  float):
          """Add a stimulus to the protocol."""
          self.stimulus.add(region, start, duration, amplitude,
  self.state.nodes)
          self._update_stimulus_tensors()

      def step(self):
          """
          Execute ONE timestep.
          
          Order matters:
          1. Apply stimulus current
          2. Advance ionic model (updates V based on Iion)
          3. Advance diffusion (spreads V spatially)
          4. Save output if needed
          5. Advance time
          """
          dt = self.config.dt
          s = self.state

          # 1. Get stimulus current
          Istim = self._compute_stimulus(s.t)

          # 2. Ionic step (modifies s.states in place)
          s.states = self.ionic_model.step(s.states, dt, Istim)

          # 3. Diffusion step (modifies voltage in s.states)
          self.time_stepper.step(s)

          # 4. Save if needed
          self._maybe_save_output()

          # 5. Advance time
          s.t = s.t + dt

      def run(
          self,
          t_end: float,
          progress_callback: Optional[Callable[[float, float], None]] = None
      ) -> Tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
          """
          Run simulation until t_end.
          
          Returns:
              times: [n_saves] - time points
              voltages: [n_saves, n_nodes] - voltage snapshots
          """
          n_steps = int(t_end / self.config.dt)

          for i in range(n_steps):
              self.step()

              if progress_callback and i % 1000 == 0:
                  progress_callback(self.state.t.item(), t_end)

          return self._collect_outputs()

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # PRIVATE HELPERS
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def _compute_stimulus(self, t: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Get stimulus current at time t."""
          return self.stimulus.get_current(t, self.state)

      def _maybe_save_output(self):
          """Save voltage to buffer if at save interval."""
          # ... buffer logic
          pass

      def _collect_outputs(self):
          """Retrieve accumulated outputs."""
          # ... return from buffer
          pass

  ---
  3. linear.py - The Equation Solver

  Purpose

  Solves Ax = b for the diffusion step using iterative methods.

  ELI5

  Given a puzzle (matrix equation), finds the answer (solution vector) by
  repeatedly guessing and improving.

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”җ
  в”Ӯ                              linear.py
   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                         "The Puzzle Solver"
   в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”ҳ

  WHAT PROBLEM IT SOLVES:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      Find x such that:  A В· x = b

      Where:
      вҖў A = (M + 0.5В·dtВ·K)   [n Г— n sparse matrix]
      вҖў b = (M - 0.5В·dtВ·K)В·V_old   [n vector]
      вҖў x = V_new   [n vector] вҶҗ what we want

      This comes from Crank-Nicolson discretization of:

          M В· dV/dt = -K В· V


  METHOD: Preconditioned Conjugate Gradient (PCG)
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      Start with guess xвӮҖ (warm start from previous solution)

      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ  ITERATION LOOP:                                                в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ    1. Compute residual:     r = b - AВ·x   "How wrong am I?"    в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ    2. Check convergence:    if ||r|| < tol: done               в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ    3. Find direction:       p = f(r)      "Which way to go?"   в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ    4. Compute step size:    Оұ = ...       "How far to go?"     в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ    5. Update solution:      x = x + ОұВ·p   "Take a step"        в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ    6. Repeat until converged (typically 30-50 iterations)      в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

      Visual:

      Error
        в”Ӯ
        в”Ӯв—Ҹ                     Start (bad guess)
        в”Ӯ в•І
        в”Ӯ  в•І                   Each iteration reduces error
        в”Ӯ   в•І
        в”Ӯ    в—Ҹ
        в”Ӯ     в•І
        в”Ӯ      в—Ҹ
        в”Ӯ       в•І___в—Ҹ___в—Ҹ      Converged (error < tolerance)
        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв–ә Iterations


  WHAT IT PROVIDES:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  вҖў solve(A, b, x0, tol, max_iter) вҶ’ x, iterations, converged
  вҖў Workspace management (pre-allocated vectors)
  вҖў Warm start support (use previous solution)

  WHAT IT DOES NOT DO:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  вң— Build matrices A, b (that's time_stepping.py)
  вң— Know about physics (just solves math)
  вң— Manage simulation state

  Code Structure

  # solver/linear.py

  import torch
  from typing import Tuple, Optional
  from dataclasses import dataclass

  @dataclass
  class PCGWorkspace:
      """Pre-allocated workspace to avoid malloc in hot loop."""
      r: torch.Tensor      # Residual
      p: torch.Tensor      # Search direction
      Ap: torch.Tensor     # Matrix-vector product A @ p
      z: torch.Tensor      # Preconditioned residual (optional)

      @classmethod
      def create(cls, n: int, device) -> 'PCGWorkspace':
          return cls(
              r=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
              p=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
              Ap=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
              z=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
          )


  class PCGSolver:
      """
      Preconditioned Conjugate Gradient solver.
      
      Solves A @ x = b for symmetric positive definite A.
      
      Features:
      - Pre-allocated workspace (no malloc during solve)
      - Warm start support (use previous solution as x0)
      - Optional preconditioning
      - Configurable convergence checking
      """

      def __init__(
          self,
          n: int,
          device,
          tol: float = 1e-8,
          max_iter: int = 500,
          check_interval: int = 1,  # How often to check convergence
      ):
          self.tol = tol
          self.max_iter = max_iter
          self.check_interval = check_interval
          self.workspace = PCGWorkspace.create(n, device)

      def solve(
          self,
          A: torch.Tensor,
          b: torch.Tensor,
          x0: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None,
      ) -> Tuple[torch.Tensor, int, bool]:
          """
          Solve A @ x = b.
          
          Args:
              A: Sparse matrix [n, n]
              b: Right-hand side [n]
              x0: Initial guess [n] (warm start)
          
          Returns:
              x: Solution [n]
              iters: Number of iterations used
              converged: Whether tolerance was reached
          """
          w = self.workspace

          # Initialize
          if x0 is not None:
              x = x0.clone()
          else:
              x = torch.zeros_like(b)

          # r = b - A @ x
          torch.sparse.mm(A, x.unsqueeze(1), out=w.Ap.unsqueeze(1))
          w.r.copy_(b).sub_(w.Ap.squeeze())

          # p = r (no preconditioning)
          w.p.copy_(w.r)

          # rsold = r @ r
          rsold = torch.dot(w.r, w.r)

          converged = False

          for i in range(self.max_iter):
              # Ap = A @ p
              torch.sparse.mm(A, w.p.unsqueeze(1), out=w.Ap.unsqueeze(1))
              w.Ap.squeeze_()

              # alpha = rsold / (p @ Ap)
              pAp = torch.dot(w.p, w.Ap)
              alpha = rsold / (pAp + 1e-30)  # Avoid division by zero

              # x = x + alpha * p
              x.add_(w.p, alpha=alpha)

              # r = r - alpha * Ap
              w.r.sub_(w.Ap, alpha=alpha)

              # rsnew = r @ r
              rsnew = torch.dot(w.r, w.r)

              # Check convergence periodically
              if i % self.check_interval == 0:
                  rnorm = torch.sqrt(rsnew).item()
                  if rnorm < self.tol:
                      converged = True
                      break

              # beta = rsnew / rsold
              beta = rsnew / (rsold + 1e-30)

              # p = r + beta * p
              w.p.mul_(beta).add_(w.r)

              rsold = rsnew

          return x, i + 1, converged


  class FixedIterPCGSolver(PCGSolver):
      """
      PCG solver with fixed iteration count (no convergence check).
      
      Use when:
      - Convergence is predictable (consistent dt)
      - Transfer overhead of .item() is costly (NVIDIA)
      """

      def __init__(self, n: int, device, fixed_iters: int = 50):
          super().__init__(n, device, max_iter=fixed_iters,
  check_interval=fixed_iters + 1)
          self.fixed_iters = fixed_iters

      def solve(self, A, b, x0=None):
          """Always runs exactly fixed_iters iterations."""
          x, _, _ = super().solve(A, b, x0)
          return x, self.fixed_iters, True  # Assume converged

  ---
  4. backend.py - The Hardware Abstraction

  Purpose

  Hides device differences (CPU/CUDA/MPS). One interface, multiple
  implementations.

  ELI5

  A translator that speaks the same language to you, but talks to different
  computers (CPU, NVIDIA GPU, Apple GPU) in their own languages.

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”җ
  в”Ӯ                              backend.py
   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                          "The Translator"
   в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  PROBLEM IT SOLVES:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      Your code says:              Backend translates to:
      в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ    в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      backend.zeros(100)     в”Җв”Җв–ә   torch.zeros(100, device='cuda')  (NVIDIA)
                             в”Җв”Җв–ә   torch.zeros(100, device='mps')   (Apple)
                             в”Җв”Җв–ә   torch.zeros(100, device='cpu')   (CPU)

      backend.sync()         в”Җв”Җв–ә   torch.cuda.synchronize()         (NVIDIA)
                             в”Җв”Җв–ә   torch.mps.synchronize()          (Apple)
                             в”Җв”Җв–ә   pass                             (CPU)


  ARCHITECTURE:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

                          в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ

  WHAT IT PROVIDES:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  вҖў Unified tensor creation (zeros, ones, tensor, linspace, etc.)
  вҖў Device detection and selection
  вҖў Synchronization primitives
  вҖў Memory management (cache clearing)
  вҖў Device info reporting

  WHAT IT DOES NOT DO:
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  вң— Physics computation
  вң— Algorithm implementation
  вң— State management

  Code Structure

  # utils/backend.py

  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
  from typing import Union, Tuple, Optional
  import torch

  class Backend(ABC):
      """
      Abstract interface for device-agnostic computation.
      
      All tensor creation and device operations go through here.
      Simulation code never calls torch.zeros() directly.
      """

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def device(self) -> torch.device:
          """The torch device this backend uses."""
          pass

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def dtype(self) -> torch.dtype:
          """Default dtype for tensors."""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def zeros(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Create zero tensor on this device."""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def ones(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Create ones tensor on this device."""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def tensor(self, data, dtype=None) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Create tensor from data on this device."""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def linspace(self, start, end, steps) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Create linspace on this device."""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def sync(self):
          """Synchronize device (wait for all operations to complete)."""
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def empty_cache(self):
          """Clear device memory cache."""
          pass

      def to_device(self, tensor: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Move tensor to this device."""
          return tensor.to(self.device, self.dtype)


  class CUDABackend(Backend):
      """Backend for NVIDIA GPUs."""

      def __init__(self, device_id: int = 0):
          self._device = torch.device(f'cuda:{device_id}')
          self._dtype = torch.float64  # CUDA supports float64 well

      @property
      def device(self) -> torch.device:
          return self._device

      @property
      def dtype(self) -> torch.dtype:
          return self._dtype

      def zeros(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.zeros(*shape, device=self._device, dtype=self._dtype)

      def ones(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.ones(*shape, device=self._device, dtype=self._dtype)

      def tensor(self, data, dtype=None) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.tensor(data, device=self._device, dtype=dtype or
  self._dtype)

      def linspace(self, start, end, steps) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.linspace(start, end, steps, device=self._device,
  dtype=self._dtype)

      def sync(self):
          torch.cuda.synchronize(self._device)

      def empty_cache(self):
          torch.cuda.empty_cache()

      def memory_allocated(self) -> int:
          return torch.cuda.memory_allocated(self._device)


  class MPSBackend(Backend):
      """Backend for Apple Silicon (M1/M2/M3/M4)."""

      def __init__(self):
          self._device = torch.device('mps')
          self._dtype = torch.float32  # MPS works best with float32

      @property
      def device(self) -> torch.device:
          return self._device

      @property
      def dtype(self) -> torch.dtype:
          return self._dtype

      def zeros(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.zeros(*shape, device=self._device, dtype=self._dtype)

      def ones(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.ones(*shape, device=self._device, dtype=self._dtype)

      def tensor(self, data, dtype=None) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.tensor(data, device=self._device, dtype=dtype or
  self._dtype)

      def linspace(self, start, end, steps) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.linspace(start, end, steps, device=self._device,
  dtype=self._dtype)

      def sync(self):
          torch.mps.synchronize()

      def empty_cache(self):
          torch.mps.empty_cache()

      def memory_allocated(self) -> int:
          # MPS doesn't have direct memory query
          return 0


  class CPUBackend(Backend):
      """Backend for CPU computation."""

      def __init__(self):
          self._device = torch.device('cpu')
          self._dtype = torch.float64

      @property
      def device(self) -> torch.device:
          return self._device

      @property
      def dtype(self) -> torch.dtype:
          return self._dtype

      def zeros(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.zeros(*shape, dtype=self._dtype)

      def ones(self, *shape) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.ones(*shape, dtype=self._dtype)

      def tensor(self, data, dtype=None) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.tensor(data, dtype=dtype or self._dtype)

      def linspace(self, start, end, steps) -> torch.Tensor:
          return torch.linspace(start, end, steps, dtype=self._dtype)

      def sync(self):
          pass  # CPU is always synchronized

      def empty_cache(self):
          pass  # No cache to clear


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # AUTO-DETECTION
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  def get_backend(device: str = 'auto') -> Backend:
      """
      Get the appropriate backend for the requested device.
      
      Args:
          device: 'auto', 'cuda', 'mps', or 'cpu'
      
      Returns:
          Backend instance for the selected device
      """
      if device == 'auto':
          if torch.cuda.is_available():
              return CUDABackend()
          elif torch.backends.mps.is_available():
              return MPSBackend()
          else:
              return CPUBackend()

      elif device == 'cuda':
          if not torch.cuda.is_available():
              raise RuntimeError("CUDA not available")
          return CUDABackend()

      elif device == 'mps':
          if not torch.backends.mps.is_available():
              raise RuntimeError("MPS not available")
          return MPSBackend()

      elif device == 'cpu':
          return CPUBackend()

      else:
          raise ValueError(f"Unknown device: {device}")


  def print_device_info():
      """Print available compute devices."""
      print("Available backends:")
      print(f"  CUDA: {torch.cuda.is_available()}")
      if torch.cuda.is_available():
          print(f"    - Device: {torch.cuda.get_device_name(0)}")
          print(f"    - Memory: 
  {torch.cuda.get_device_properties(0).total_memory / 1e9:.1f} GB")
      print(f"  MPS:  {torch.backends.mps.is_available()}")
      print(f"  CPU:  Always available")

  ---

вқҜ where ionicModel.step found 

вҸә In our proposed architecture, IonicModel.step() lives in the ionic layer:

  cardiac_sim/
  в””в”Җв”Җ ionic/
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ base.py                    вҶҗ IonicModel ABC (interface definition)
      в””в”Җв”Җ models/
          в”ңв”Җв”Җ ord/
          в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ model.py           вҶҗ ORdModel.step() (41-state implementation)
          в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ gating.py          вҶҗ called by step()
          в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ currents.py        вҶҗ called by step()
          в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ calcium.py         вҶҗ called by step()
          в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ camkii.py         вҶҗ called by step()
          в””в”Җв”Җ ttp06/
              в”ңв”Җв”Җ model.py           вҶҗ TTP06Model.step() (19-state
  implementation)
              в”ңв”Җв”Җ gating.py          вҶҗ called by step()
              в”ңв”Җв”Җ currents.py        вҶҗ called by step()
              в””в”Җв”Җ calcium.py         вҶҗ called by step()

  ---
  Two layers to it

  1. ionic/base.py вҖ” The Interface (what step must look like)

  # ionic/base.py

  class IonicModel(ABC):
      """Every ionic model must implement these methods."""

      @abstractmethod
      def step(self, states: torch.Tensor, dt: float, Istim: torch.Tensor) -> 
  torch.Tensor:
          """
          Advance all cells by one timestep.
          
          Args:
              states: [n_nodes, n_states] - all state variables
              dt:     timestep (ms)
              Istim:  [n_nodes] - stimulus current per node
          
          Returns:
              states: [n_nodes, n_states] - updated states
          """
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def compute_Iion(self, states: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          pass

      @abstractmethod
      def get_initial_state(self, n_cells: int) -> torch.Tensor:
          pass

  2. ionic/models/ttp06/model.py вҖ” The Implementation (what step actually does)

  # ionic/models/ttp06/model.py

  class TTP06Model(IonicModel):

      def step(self, states, dt, Istim):
          """
          One timestep of the TTP06 model.
          Coordinates calls to gating, currents, calcium.
          """
          V = states[:, 0]

          # 1. Update gates (Rush-Larsen) в”Җв”Җв–ә gating.py
          states = update_gates(states, V, dt)

          # 2. Compute ionic currents в”Җв”Җв–ә currents.py
          Iion = compute_currents(states, V, self.params)

          # 3. Update voltage (Forward Euler)
          states[:, 0] = V + dt * (-Iion + Istim)

          # 4. Update calcium в”Җв”Җв–ә calcium.py
          states = update_calcium(states, dt, Iion_components)

          return states

  ---

  sim.step()
    в”Ӯ
    в”ңв”Җв”Җ Istim = stimulus.get_current()
    в”Ӯ
    в”ңв”Җв”Җ state.states = self.ionic_model.step(state.states, dt, Istim)
    в”Ӯ                         в”Ӯ

    в”Ӯ                         в”Ӯ        в”Ӯ

    в”Ӯ                  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
    в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ  ttp06/model.py  step()  в”Ӯ
    в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ         в”Ӯ                в”Ӯ
    в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ    в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҙв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ           в”Ӯ
    в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ    в–ј    в–ј    в–ј           в”Ӯ
    в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ  gating currents calcium в”Ӯ
    в”Ӯ                  в”Ӯ  .py    .py     .py      в”Ӯ
    в”Ӯ                  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
    в”Ӯ
    в”ңв”Җв”Җ time_stepper.step(state)   в”Җв”Җв–ә diffusion
    в”Ӯ
    ...

  monodomain.py never sees gating.py, currents.py, or calcium.py. It only calls
  ionic_model.step() and the model handles its own internals. That's the point
  of the IonicModel interface in base.py вҖ” monodomain doesn't care whether it's
  TTP06 (19 states) or ORd (41 states), it just calls .step().

вқҜ i would recommend pulling the step function out from the ionic models/    
  and putting into a dedicated place in the simulaiton folder. all          
  funcitons in ionic just provides the necessiary calls needed to perform   
  each step.                                                                

вҸә That's a solid design choice. It separates what the cell knows (ion channel
  physics) from how the simulation uses it (stepping strategy). Here's how that
  restructures things:

  Current vs Your Proposal

  CURRENT: step() lives inside ionic model
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  ionic/models/ttp06/model.py
  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ  class TTP06Model:              в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                 в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    step()          в—„в”Җв”Җ orchestration logic lives here
  в”Ӯ    compute_Iion()               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    get_initial_state()          в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    update_gates()               в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    update_calcium()             в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  Problem: The model knows HOW to step itself.
           Mixing physics data with simulation strategy.


  YOUR PROPOSAL: step() lives in simulation/
  в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  ionic/models/ttp06/model.py             simulation/integrators.py
  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ     в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
  в”Ӯ  class TTP06Model:              в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ  class IonicIntegrator:         в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                 в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ                                 в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    compute_Iion()               в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ    step()  в—„в”Җв”Җ orchestration   в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    compute_gates()              в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ    ionic_step()                в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    compute_calcium()            в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ    diffusion_step()            в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    get_initial_state()          в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ                                 в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ                                 в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ    Calls ionic model functions  в”Ӯ
  в”Ӯ    Provides DATA only           в”Ӯ     в”Ӯ    to perform each step         в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ     в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  Ionic model: "Here are my currents, gates, calcium dynamics"
  Integrator:  "I decide the order and method to advance them"

  ---
  Why This Is Better

  SEPARATION OF CONCERNS:

      ionic/                          simulation/
      в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ                          в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      WHAT the cell does              HOW to advance it
      в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ               в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      "INa = gNaВ·mВіВ·hВ·jВ·(V-ENa)"    "Use Rush-Larsen for gates"
      "ICaL = ..."                    "Use Forward Euler for calcium"
      "dCa/dt = fluxes"              "Apply stimulus before Iion"
                                      "Do ionic before diffusion"

      Physics knowledge               Numerical knowledge
      Model-specific                   Reusable across models
      Changes when biology changes     Changes when numerics change

  Key advantage вҖ” you can swap stepping strategy without touching ionic models:

  SAME ionic model, DIFFERENT stepping strategies:

      TTP06Model в”Җв”Җв–ә ForwardEulerIntegrator     (simple, fast)
      TTP06Model в”Җв”Җв–ә RushLarsenIntegrator       (standard, stable)
      TTP06Model в”Җв”Җв–ә AdaptiveDTIntegrator       (variable timestep)
      TTP06Model в”Җв”Җв–ә StrangSplitIntegrator      (2nd order splitting)

  ---
  Revised Architecture

  cardiac_sim/
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ base.py                    # IonicModel ABC (data interface only)
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ models/
  в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ ord/
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ model.py           # ORdModel - provides gate/current/calcium
  functions
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ parameters.py
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ gating.py          # compute_gate_inf(), compute_gate_tau()
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ currents.py        # compute_INa(), compute_ICaL(), ...
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ calcium.py         # compute_calcium_fluxes()
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ camkii.py         # compute_camkii()
  в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ ttp06/
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ model.py           # TTP06Model - provides
  gate/current/calcium functions
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ parameters.py
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ gating.py
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ currents.py
  в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ calcium.py
  в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ lut.py
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ simulation/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ state.py                   # SimulationState (data container)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ monodomain.py              # MonodomainSimulation (top-level
  orchestrator)
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ integrators.py             # IonicIntegrator вҶҗ step() LIVES HERE
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ stimulus.py                # StimulusProtocol
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ tissue/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ...
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ solver/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ...
  в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җ utils/
      в””в”Җв”Җ backend.py

  ---
  Revised ionic/base.py вҖ” Data Provider Only

  # ionic/base.py
  # The model only PROVIDES computation functions.
  # It does NOT decide how or when they are called.

  class IonicModel(ABC):
      """
      Interface for ionic models.
      
      Models provide FUNCTIONS for computing quantities.
      Models do NOT control stepping order or numerical method.
      """

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # IDENTITY
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def name(self) -> str: ...

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def n_states(self) -> int: ...

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def V_index(self) -> int: ...

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def gate_indices(self) -> List[int]:
          """Which state indices are gating variables (for Rush-Larsen)."""
          ...

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def concentration_indices(self) -> List[int]:
          """Which state indices are concentrations (for Forward Euler)."""
          ...

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # INITIALIZATION
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      @abstractmethod
      def get_initial_state(self, n_cells: int) -> torch.Tensor: ...

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # COMPUTATION FUNCTIONS (called by integrator)
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      @abstractmethod
      def compute_Iion(self, states: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Total ionic current. Called by integrator."""
          ...

      @abstractmethod
      def compute_gate_steady_states(self, V: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Gate infinity values: m_inf, h_inf, etc. For Rush-Larsen."""
          ...

      @abstractmethod
      def compute_gate_time_constants(self, V: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Gate time constants: tau_m, tau_h, etc. For Rush-Larsen."""
          ...

      @abstractmethod
      def compute_concentration_rates(self, states: torch.Tensor) -> 
  torch.Tensor:
          """dC/dt for all concentrations. For Forward Euler."""
          ...

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # CONVENIENCE (optional)
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def get_voltage(self, states: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          return states[..., self.V_index]

      def set_voltage(self, states: torch.Tensor, V: torch.Tensor):
          states[..., self.V_index] = V

  ---
  New simulation/integrators.py вҖ” Step Logic Lives Here

  # simulation/integrators.py
  # ALL stepping logic is here, not in ionic models.

  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
  import torch
  from ..ionic.base import IonicModel

  class IonicIntegrator(ABC):
      """
      Base class for ionic time integration.
      
      Decides HOW to advance the ionic model:
      - What numerical method for gates (Rush-Larsen, Euler, etc.)
      - What numerical method for concentrations
      - What order to compute things
      """

      @abstractmethod
      def step(
          self,
          model: IonicModel,
          states: torch.Tensor,
          dt: float,
          Istim: torch.Tensor
      ) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Advance ionic state by dt."""
          ...


  class RushLarsenIntegrator(IonicIntegrator):
      """
      Standard cardiac integration:
      - Rush-Larsen (exponential) for gating variables
      - Forward Euler for concentrations
      - Forward Euler for voltage
      """

      def step(self, model, states, dt, Istim):
          V = model.get_voltage(states)

          # 1. Gates: Rush-Larsen (exponential integration)
          g_inf = model.compute_gate_steady_states(V)      # Where gates want to
   be
          g_tau = model.compute_gate_time_constants(V)      # How fast they get 
  there

          gate_idx = model.gate_indices
          for i, idx in enumerate(gate_idx):
              g_old = states[:, idx]
              states[:, idx] = g_inf[:, i] - (g_inf[:, i] - g_old) *
  torch.exp(-dt / g_tau[:, i])

          # 2. Ionic current (uses updated gates, old V)
          Iion = model.compute_Iion(states)

          # 3. Voltage: Forward Euler
          dVdt = -Iion + Istim
          model.set_voltage(states, V + dt * dVdt)

          # 4. Concentrations: Forward Euler
          dCdt = model.compute_concentration_rates(states)

          conc_idx = model.concentration_indices
          for i, idx in enumerate(conc_idx):
              states[:, idx] = states[:, idx] + dt * dCdt[:, i]

          return states


  class ForwardEulerIntegrator(IonicIntegrator):
      """
      Simple Forward Euler for everything.
      Less stable, but simpler. Good for testing.
      """

      def step(self, model, states, dt, Istim):
          V = model.get_voltage(states)

          # All gates by Euler (less stable than Rush-Larsen)
          g_inf = model.compute_gate_steady_states(V)
          g_tau = model.compute_gate_time_constants(V)

          gate_idx = model.gate_indices
          for i, idx in enumerate(gate_idx):
              g_old = states[:, idx]
              dgdt = (g_inf[:, i] - g_old) / g_tau[:, i]
              states[:, idx] = g_old + dt * dgdt

          Iion = model.compute_Iion(states)

          dVdt = -Iion + Istim
          model.set_voltage(states, V + dt * dVdt)

          dCdt = model.compute_concentration_rates(states)
          conc_idx = model.concentration_indices
          for i, idx in enumerate(conc_idx):
              states[:, idx] = states[:, idx] + dt * dCdt[:, i]

          return states


  class AdaptiveDTIntegrator(IonicIntegrator):
      """
      Adaptive timestep integration.
      Takes smaller steps during rapid depolarization,
      larger steps during plateau/resting.
      """

      def __init__(self, dt_min: float = 0.001, dt_max: float = 0.1, tol: float 
  = 0.5):
          self.dt_min = dt_min
          self.dt_max = dt_max
          self.tol = tol  # mV error tolerance
          self.rush_larsen = RushLarsenIntegrator()

      def step(self, model, states, dt, Istim):
          V_old = model.get_voltage(states).clone()

          # Full step
          states_full = self.rush_larsen.step(model, states.clone(), dt, Istim)

          # Two half steps
          states_half = self.rush_larsen.step(model, states.clone(), dt/2,
  Istim)
          states_half = self.rush_larsen.step(model, states_half, dt/2, Istim)

          # Error estimate
          V_full = model.get_voltage(states_full)
          V_half = model.get_voltage(states_half)
          error = torch.max(torch.abs(V_full - V_half)).item()

          if error < self.tol:
              return states_half  # Accept half-step result (more accurate)
          else:
              # Reject and retry with smaller dt
              return self.step(model, states, dt / 2, Istim)

  Updated simulation/monodomain.py

  # simulation/monodomain.py
  # Now uses integrator instead of calling model.step() directly

  class MonodomainSimulation:

      def __init__(self, mesh, ionic_model, config, backend):
          self.ionic_model = ionic_model
          self.backend = backend
          self.config = config

          # State container
          self.state = create_state(mesh, ionic_model, config, backend.device)

          # IONIC integrator (swappable!)
          self.ionic_integrator = config.ionic_integrator  # e.g., 
  RushLarsenIntegrator()

          # DIFFUSION solver
          self.time_stepper = CrankNicolsonStepper(...)

          # Stimulus
          self.stimulus = StimulusProtocol(device=backend.device)

      def step(self):
          dt = self.config.dt
          s = self.state

          # 1. Stimulus
          Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(s.t, s)

          # 2. Ionic step вҖ” integrator calls model's compute functions
          s.states = self.ionic_integrator.step(
              model=self.ionic_model,   # provides compute_Iion, compute_gates, 
  etc.
              states=s.states,
              dt=dt,
              Istim=Istim
          )

          # 3. Diffusion step
          self.time_stepper.step(s)

          # 4. Save & advance
          self._maybe_save_output()
          s.t = s.t + dt

  ---
  The Key File: simulation/step.py

  Purpose

  Combines ionic + diffusion solvers using a splitting strategy. This is where
  you swap between Godunov (1st order) and Strang (2nd order).

  в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

   в”Ӯ

  в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

      Godunov (1st order):              Strang (2nd order):
      в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ              в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ              в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ  Full ionic step в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ  Half ionic step в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ     (dt)         в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ     (dt/2)       в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ              в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ
               в”Ӯ                                 в”Ӯ
               в–ј                                 в–ј
      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ              в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ Full diffusion   в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ Full diffusion   в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ     (dt)         в”Ӯ              в”Ӯ     (dt)         в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ              в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”¬в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

                                        в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

                                                 Error: O(dtВІ)

  Code

  # simulation/step.py

  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
  from .solvers.ionic_solver import IonicSolver
  from .solvers.diffusion_solver import DiffusionSolver
  from .state import SimulationState
  from .stimulus import StimulusProtocol


  class StepCoordinator(ABC):
      """
      Combines ionic and diffusion solvers into one complete timestep.
      
      This is the ONLY place that knows about splitting strategy.
      Swapping Godunov for Strang happens HERE, not in monodomain.py
      and not in either solver.
      """

      def __init__(
          self,
          ionic_solver: IonicSolver,
          diffusion_solver: DiffusionSolver,
          stimulus: StimulusProtocol,
      ):
          self.ionic_solver = ionic_solver
          self.diffusion_solver = diffusion_solver
          self.stimulus = stimulus

      @abstractmethod
      def step(self, state: SimulationState, model, dt: float):
          """Execute one complete timestep."""
          ...


  class GodunovSplitting(StepCoordinator):
      """
      First-order operator splitting.
      
          V^{n+1} = D(dt) В· I(dt) В· V^n
      
      Error: O(dt)
      Cost:  1 ionic solve + 1 diffusion solve
      """

      def step(self, state, model, dt):
          # 1. Full ionic step
          Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.states, dt, Istim)

          # 2. Full diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, dt)

          # 3. Advance time
          state.t = state.t + dt


  class StrangSplitting(StepCoordinator):
      """
      Second-order operator splitting.
      
          V^{n+1} = I(dt/2) В· D(dt) В· I(dt/2) В· V^n
      
      Error: O(dtВІ)
      Cost:  2 ionic solves (half step each) + 1 diffusion solve
      """

      def step(self, state, model, dt):
          half_dt = dt / 2.0

          # 1. Half ionic step
          Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.states, half_dt,
  Istim)

          # 2. Full diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, dt)

          # 3. Half ionic step
          Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.states, half_dt,
  Istim)

          # 4. Advance time
          state.t = state.t + dt


  class SymmetricStrangSplitting(StepCoordinator):
      """
      Symmetric Strang: diffusion-ionic-diffusion order.
      
          V^{n+1} = D(dt/2) В· I(dt) В· D(dt/2) В· V^n
      
      Error: O(dtВІ)
      Sometimes better if diffusion is the stiffer operator.
      """

      def step(self, state, model, dt):
          half_dt = dt / 2.0

          # 1. Half diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, half_dt)

          # 2. Full ionic step
          Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.states, dt, Istim)

          # 3. Half diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, half_dt)

          # 4. Advance time
          state.t = state.t + dt

  Updated Solvers (Renamed)

  simulation/solvers/ionic_solver.py

  # simulation/solvers/ionic_solver.py
  # Renamed from integrators.py. Only handles ionic ODE advancement.

  class IonicSolver(ABC):
      """Advances ionic ODEs. Does NOT know about diffusion or splitting."""

      @abstractmethod
      def solve(self, model, states, dt, Istim) -> torch.Tensor:
          ...


  class RushLarsenSolver(IonicSolver):
      """Rush-Larsen for gates, Forward Euler for concentrations."""

      def solve(self, model, states, dt, Istim):
          V = model.get_voltage(states)

          # Gates: exponential integration
          g_inf = model.compute_gate_steady_states(V)
          g_tau = model.compute_gate_time_constants(V)

          for i, idx in enumerate(model.gate_indices):
              g_old = states[:, idx]
              states[:, idx] = g_inf[:, i] - (g_inf[:, i] - g_old) *
  torch.exp(-dt / g_tau[:, i])

          # Current
          Iion = model.compute_Iion(states)

          # Voltage
          model.set_voltage(states, V + dt * (-Iion + Istim))

          # Concentrations
          dCdt = model.compute_concentration_rates(states)
          for i, idx in enumerate(model.concentration_indices):
              states[:, idx] += dt * dCdt[:, i]

          return states


  class ForwardEulerSolver(IonicSolver):
      """Simple Euler for everything. Testing/comparison."""

      def solve(self, model, states, dt, Istim):
          ...

  simulation/solvers/diffusion_solver.py

  # simulation/solvers/diffusion_solver.py
  # Renamed from time_stepping.py. Only handles spatial diffusion.

  class DiffusionSolver(ABC):
      """Solves the diffusion PDE. Does NOT know about ionic models."""

      @abstractmethod
      def solve(self, state: SimulationState, dt: float):
          ...


  class CrankNicolsonDiffusion(DiffusionSolver):
      """
      Crank-Nicolson scheme for diffusion.
      Solves: (M + 0.5В·dtВ·K)В·V_new = (M - 0.5В·dtВ·K)В·V_old
      """

      def __init__(self, pcg_solver, M, K):
          self.pcg = pcg_solver
          self.M = M
          self.K = K
          self._cached_dt = None
          self._A = None  # LHS matrix
          self._B = None  # RHS matrix

      def solve(self, state, dt):
          # Cache matrices for fixed dt
          if dt != self._cached_dt:
              self._A = self.M + 0.5 * dt * self.K
              self._B = self.M - 0.5 * dt * self.K
              self._cached_dt = dt

          V = state.states[:, 0]

          # b = B @ V
          b = torch.sparse.mm(self._B, V.unsqueeze(1)).squeeze()

          # Solve A @ V_new = b
          V_new, iters, converged = self.pcg.solve(self._A, b, state.pcg_x)

          # Update
          state.states[:, 0] = V_new
          state.pcg_x = V_new  # Warm start for next step


  class BDF1Diffusion(DiffusionSolver):
      """Backward Euler (BDF1). L-stable, 1st order."""

      def solve(self, state, dt):
          ...


  class BDF2Diffusion(DiffusionSolver):
      """BDF2. A-stable, 2nd order. Requires two previous solutions."""

      def solve(self, state, dt):
          ...

  Updated simulation/monodomain.py вҖ” Now Clean

  # simulation/monodomain.py
  # Thin orchestration layer. All logic delegated.

  class MonodomainSimulation:
      """
      Top-level API. User-facing.
      
      All it does:
      1. Initialize components
      2. Call step_coordinator.step() in a loop
      3. Collect outputs
      """

      def __init__(self, mesh, ionic_model, config, backend):
          self.ionic_model = ionic_model
          self.config = config

          # State
          self.state = create_state(mesh, ionic_model, config, backend.device)

          # Build solvers
          pcg = PCGSolver(n=mesh.n_nodes, device=backend.device,
  **config.pcg_params)
          ionic_solver = config.ionic_solver       # e.g., RushLarsenSolver()
          diffusion_solver = config.diffusion_solver(pcg, self.state.M,
  self.state.K)
          stimulus = StimulusProtocol(device=backend.device)

          # Step coordinator (splitting strategy)
          self.stepper = config.splitting_strategy(
              ionic_solver=ionic_solver,
              diffusion_solver=diffusion_solver,
              stimulus=stimulus,
          )

      def add_stimulus(self, region, start, duration, amplitude):
          self.stepper.stimulus.add(region, start, duration, amplitude,
  self.state.nodes)

      def step(self):
          self.stepper.step(self.state, self.ionic_model, self.config.dt)

      def run(self, t_end, progress_callback=None):
          n_steps = int(t_end / self.config.dt)

          for i in range(n_steps):
              self.step()
              self._maybe_save()

              if progress_callback and i % 1000 == 0:
                  progress_callback(self.state.t.item(), t_end)

          return self._collect_outputs()

  Swapping Strategies вҖ” User's Perspective

  from cardiac_sim.simulation import MonodomainSimulation
  from cardiac_sim.simulation.step import GodunovSplitting, StrangSplitting
  from cardiac_sim.simulation.solvers.ionic_solver import RushLarsenSolver
  from cardiac_sim.simulation.solvers.diffusion_solver import
  CrankNicolsonDiffusion

  config = SimulationConfig(
      dt=0.02,

      # Swap these independently:
      ionic_solver=RushLarsenSolver(),               # or ForwardEulerSolver()
      diffusion_solver=CrankNicolsonDiffusion,       # or BDF1Diffusion, 
  BDF2Diffusion
      splitting_strategy=StrangSplitting,            # or GodunovSplitting
  )

  sim = MonodomainSimulation(mesh, model, config, backend)
  sim.run(t_end=500.0)

  diffusion

вҸә Let me think through this carefully.

  Proposed Structure

  simulation/
  в””в”Җв”Җ solvers/
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ solver_functions.py      # Rush-Larsen, Forward Euler math
      в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ integrator.py            # IonicSolver classes
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ diffusion/
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ solver_functions.py      # PCG, matrix ops
      в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ integrator.py            # DiffusionSolver classes
      в””в”Җв”Җ (linear.py absorbed into diffusion/)

  Assessment: Mixed

  There are merits, but also a structural problem. Let me lay both out.

  What works

  GOOD: Compartmentalizing ionic/ vs diffusion/

      solvers/
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/           вҶҗ everything about advancing ODEs
      в””в”Җв”Җ diffusion/       вҶҗ everything about advancing PDEs

      Clear separation. Easy to navigate.

  What doesn't work

  The solver_functions.py + integrator.py split creates an artificial boundary
  inside each folder:

  PROBLEM: What goes where?

      ionic/
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ solver_functions.py     # exp(-dt/tau)?  (m_inf - m) * exp()?
      в”Ӯ                           # The full Rush-Larsen formula?
      в”Ӯ                           # Or just the exponential part?
      в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җ integrator.py           # Calls solver_functions?
                                  # But the integration IS the function.


      Rush-Larsen IS one line:
      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ  m_new = m_inf - (m_inf - m_old) * exp(-dt / tau)           в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ           в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  Which file does this belong to?                             в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  solver_functions.py? integrator.py? It's both.             в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ


      Same problem on diffusion side:
      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ  solver_functions.py:  PCG iteration loop                   в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  integrator.py:        Build A, b, call PCG                 в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ                                                             в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  But integrator.py is just 5 lines wrapping                в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  solver_functions.py. Two files for one concept.            в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ

  ---
  Counter-Proposal

  Keep the ionic/ and diffusion/ compartments (that's good), but split by what 
  changes independently, not by abstraction level:

  simulation/
  в””в”Җв”Җ solvers/
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ __init__.py
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ rush_larsen.py          # RushLarsenSolver class + its math
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ forward_euler.py        # ForwardEulerSolver class + its math
      в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adaptive.py             # AdaptiveDTSolver class + its math
      в”Ӯ
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ diffusion/
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ __init__.py
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ crank_nicolson.py       # CrankNicolsonSolver class + matrix build
   + PCG call
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ bdf1.py                 # BDF1Solver class
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ bdf2.py                 # BDF2Solver class
      в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ pcg.py                  # PCGSolver (pure linear algebra, shared)
      в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җ __init__.py                 # Re-exports: IonicSolver, DiffusionSolver
   ABCs

  Why one-file-per-method is better

  SCENARIO: Adding a new ionic solver (e.g., Hybrid IMEX)

      solver_functions + integrator approach:
      в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
      в”Ӯ  1. Add functions to solver_functions.py (file grows)       в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  2. Add class to integrator.py (file grows)                в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  3. Both files now have Rush-Larsen + Euler + IMEX code    в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ  4. Hard to find what belongs to what                      в”Ӯ

      Advances ionic ODEs by one timestep.
      Subclasses implement specific numerical methods.
      """

      @abstractmethod
      def solve(
          self,
          model: IonicModel,
          states: torch.Tensor,
          dt: float,
          Istim: torch.Tensor

  solvers/ionic/rush_larsen.py вҖ” Self-Contained

  # simulation/solvers/ionic/rush_larsen.py

  import torch
  from . import IonicSolver

  class RushLarsenSolver(IonicSolver):
      """
      Rush-Larsen exponential integration for gates.
      Forward Euler for concentrations and voltage.
      
      Method:
          gate_new = g_inf - (g_inf - g_old) * exp(-dt / tau)
          V_new    = V_old + dt * (-Iion + Istim)
          C_new    = C_old + dt * dCdt
      """

      def solve(self, model, states, dt, Istim):
          V = model.get_voltage(states)

          # --- Gates: Rush-Larsen ---
          g_inf = model.compute_gate_steady_states(V)
          g_tau = model.compute_gate_time_constants(V)
          exp_factor = torch.exp(-dt / g_tau)

          for i, idx in enumerate(model.gate_indices):
              states[:, idx] = g_inf[:, i] - (g_inf[:, i] - states[:, idx]) *
  exp_factor[:, i]

          # --- Current ---
          Iion = model.compute_Iion(states)

          # --- Voltage: Forward Euler ---
          model.set_voltage(states, V + dt * (-Iion + Istim))

          # --- Concentrations: Forward Euler ---
          dCdt = model.compute_concentration_rates(states)
          for i, idx in enumerate(model.concentration_indices):
              states[:, idx] += dt * dCdt[:, i]

          return states

  solvers/diffusion/pcg.py вҖ” Pure Linear Algebra

  # simulation/solvers/diffusion/pcg.py

  import torch
  from dataclasses import dataclass

  @dataclass
  class PCGWorkspace:
      r: torch.Tensor
      p: torch.Tensor
      Ap: torch.Tensor

      @classmethod
      def create(cls, n, device):
          return cls(
              r=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
              p=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
              Ap=torch.zeros(n, device=device),
          )


  class PCGSolver:
      """
      Preconditioned Conjugate Gradient.
      Solves A @ x = b for symmetric positive definite A.
      
      Pure math. Knows nothing about physics.
      """

      def __init__(self, n, device, tol=1e-8, max_iter=500, check_interval=1):
          self.tol = tol
          self.max_iter = max_iter
          self.check_interval = check_interval
          self.ws = PCGWorkspace.create(n, device)

      def solve(self, A, b, x0=None):
          """Returns (x, iterations, converged)."""
          ...

  solvers/diffusion/crank_nicolson.py вҖ” Self-Contained

  # simulation/solvers/diffusion/crank_nicolson.py

  import torch
  from . import DiffusionSolver
  from .pcg import PCGSolver

  class CrankNicolsonSolver(DiffusionSolver):
      """
      Crank-Nicolson implicit scheme for diffusion.
      
      Solves: (M + 0.5В·dtВ·K) В· V_new = (M - 0.5В·dtВ·K) В· V_old
      
      2nd order accurate, unconditionally stable.
      """

      def __init__(self, M, K, pcg: PCGSolver):
          self.M = M
          self.K = K
          self.pcg = pcg
          self._cached_dt = None
          self._A = None
          self._B = None

      def _build_matrices(self, dt):
          if dt != self._cached_dt:
              self._A = self.M + 0.5 * dt * self.K
              self._B = self.M - 0.5 * dt * self.K
              self._cached_dt = dt

      def solve(self, state, dt):
          self._build_matrices(dt)

          V = state.states[:, 0]
          b = torch.sparse.mm(self._B, V.unsqueeze(1)).squeeze()

          V_new, iters, converged = self.pcg.solve(self._A, b, state.pcg_x)

          state.states[:, 0] = V_new
          state.pcg_x = V_new

  Verdict

  Your instinct to compartmentalize ionic/ and diffusion/ is correct. Absorbing
  linear.py into diffusion/pcg.py is also correct вҖ” PCG only exists to serve
  diffusion. The refinement is: one file per method instead of
  solver_functions.py + integrator.py, because the function and the integrator
  are the same concept.

  Want me to document this final architecture in improvement.md?

          -ture)
