      130  
      113 -## Side-by-Side Comparison                                    
      131 +## Design Principles                                          
      132  
      115 -| Aspect | Current | Proposed | Improvement |                 
      116 -|--------|---------|----------|-------------|                 
      117 -| **Mesh location** | `fem/mesh.py` | `tissue/mesh.py` | Group
          -s spatial concerns together |                                 
      118 -| **Discretization** | FEM only | FEM/FDM/FVM pluggable | Exte
          -nsible to new methods |                                       
      119 -| **LUT location** | `ionic/lut.py` | `ionic/models/lut.py` | 
          -Co-located with models it serves |                            
      120 -| **Simulation** | Inside `tissue/` | Top-level `simulation/` 
          -| Clear entry point, separation of concerns |                 
      121 -| **Future models** | Flat in `ionic/` | Nested in `ionic/mode
          -ls/` | Scalable organization |                                
      122 -| **Operator splitting** | Implicit in simulation | Explicit i
          -n `solver/` | Reusable, testable |                            
      133 +### 1. Physics vs Numerics vs Hardware                        
      134  
      135 +```                                                           
      136 +                        Biology   Numerics   Hardware   Data  
      137 +                        в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ  
      138 +ionic/models/             вң“                                   
      139 +simulation/solvers/                  вң“                        
      140 +simulation/step.py                   вң“                        
          +(splitting order)                                             
      141 +simulation/monodomain.py                                      
          +(orchestration)                                               
      142 +simulation/state.py                                     вң“     
      143 +utils/backend.py                                вң“             
      144 +```                                                           
      145 +                                                              
      146 +### 2. Ionic Models Are Data Providers Only                   
      147 +                                                              
      148 +Models provide **computation functions**. They do not control 
          +stepping strategy.                                            
      149 +                                                              
      150 +```                                                           
      151 +ionic/base.py defines:              Simulation decides:       
      152 +в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ               в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ        
      153 +compute_Iion()                      When to call Iion         
      154 +compute_gate_steady_states()        Rush-Larsen or Euler for g
          +ates                                                          
      155 +compute_gate_time_constants()       dt size and substep count 
      156 +compute_concentration_rates()       Splitting order           
      157 +get_initial_state()                 Godunov or Strang         
      158 +```                                                           
      159 +                                                              
      160 +### 3. One File Per Solver Method                             
      161 +                                                              
      162 +Each solver is self-contained in a single file. Adding a new s
          +olver means adding one file вҖ” no existing files change.       
      163 +                                                              
      164 +```                                                           
      165 +Adding a new ionic solver (e.g., Hybrid IMEX):                
      166 +                                                              
      167 +    1. Create solvers/ionic/hybrid_imex.py                    
      168 +    2. Implement IonicSolver ABC                              
      169 +    3. Done. Other files untouched.                           
      170 +                                                              
      171 +Adding a new diffusion solver (e.g., explicit method):        
      172 +                                                              
      173 +    1. Create solvers/diffusion/explicit.py                   
      174 +    2. Implement DiffusionSolver ABC                          
      175 +    3. Done. Other files untouched.                           
      176 +```                                                           
      177 +                                                              
      178  ---
      179  
      180 +## Core Files Explained                                       
      181 +                                                              
      182 +### `simulation/state.py` вҖ” The Data Container                
      183 +                                                              
      184 +Holds ALL simulation data in one place. Single source of truth
          +. No algorithms вҖ” pure data.                                  
      185 +                                                              
      186 +```                                                           
      187 +SimulationState contains:                                     
      188 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ states[n_nodes, n_states]         # V, gates, concentratio
          +ns                                                            
      189 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ t                                 # Current simulation tim
          +e                                                             
      190 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ nodes[n_nodes, 2]                 # Mesh coordinates      
      191 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ elements[n_elem, 3]              # Triangle connectivity  
      192 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ M, K, A, B                       # FEM matrices (sparse)  
      193 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ stim_masks, stim_times, stim_amps # Precomputed stimulus  
      194 +в”ңв”Җв”Җ pcg_r, pcg_p, pcg_Ap, pcg_x      # Solver workspace       
      195 +в””в”Җв”Җ output_buffer, buffer_idx         # Saved snapshots       
      196 +```                                                           
      197 +                                                              
      198 +### `simulation/monodomain.py` вҖ” The Top-Level API            
      199 +                                                              
      200 +User-facing orchestrator. Initializes components, runs the loo
          +p, collects outputs. Delegates all computation.               
      201 +                                                              
      202 +```python                                                     
      203 +class MonodomainSimulation:                                   
      204 +    def __init__(self, mesh, ionic_model, config, backend):   
      205 +        self.state = create_state(mesh, ionic_model, config, b
          +ackend.device)                                                
      206 +        self.stepper = config.splitting_strategy(             
      207 +            ionic_solver=config.ionic_solver,                 
      208 +            diffusion_solver=config.diffusion_solver(pcg, M, K
          +),                                                            
      209 +            stimulus=StimulusProtocol(device=backend.device), 
      210 +        )                                                     
      211 +                                                              
      212 +    def step(self):                                           
      213 +        self.stepper.step(self.state, self.ionic_model, self.c
          +onfig.dt)                                                     
      214 +                                                              
      215 +    def run(self, t_end):                                     
      216 +        for i in range(int(t_end / self.config.dt)):          
      217 +            self.step()                                       
      218 +            self._maybe_save()                                
      219 +        return self._collect_outputs()                        
      220 +```                                                           
      221 +                                                              
      222 +### `simulation/step.py` вҖ” Splitting Strategies               
      223 +                                                              
      224 +Combines ionic + diffusion solvers. This is where Godunov vs S
          +trang is decided.                                             
      225 +                                                              
      226 +```python                                                     
      227 +class GodunovSplitting(StepCoordinator):                      
      228 +    """1st order: ionic(dt) вҶ’ diffusion(dt). Error O(dt)."""  
      229 +    def step(self, state, model, dt):                         
      230 +        Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)              
      231 +        state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.st
          +ates, dt, Istim)                                              
      232 +        self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, dt)                
      233 +        state.t = state.t + dt                                
      234 +                                                              
      235 +class StrangSplitting(StepCoordinator):                       
      236 +    """2nd order: ionic(dt/2) вҶ’ diffusion(dt) вҶ’ ionic(dt/2). E
          +rror O(dtВІ)."""                                               
      237 +    def step(self, state, model, dt):                         
      238 +        half = dt / 2.0                                       
      239 +        Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)              
      240 +        state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.st
          +ates, half, Istim)                                            
      241 +        self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, dt)                
      242 +        Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)              
      243 +        state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.st
          +ates, half, Istim)                                            
      244 +        state.t = state.t + dt                                
      245 +                                                              
      246 +class SymmetricStrangSplitting(StepCoordinator):              
      247 +    """2nd order: diffusion(dt/2) вҶ’ ionic(dt) вҶ’ diffusion(dt/2
          +). Error O(dtВІ)."""                                           
      248 +    def step(self, state, model, dt):                         
      249 +        half = dt / 2.0                                       
      250 +        self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, half)              
      251 +        Istim = self.stimulus.get_current(state)              
      252 +        state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(model, state.st
          +ates, dt, Istim)                                              
      253 +        self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, half)              
      254 +        state.t = state.t + dt                                
      255 +```                                                           
      256 +                                                              
      257 +### `simulation/solvers/ionic/` вҖ” Ionic ODE Solvers           
      258 +                                                              
      259 +Each file is one self-contained solver method.                
      260 +                                                              
      261 +**`rush_larsen.py`** вҖ” Rush-Larsen exponential for gates, Forw
          +ard Euler for concentrations:                                 
      262 +```python                                                     
      263 +class RushLarsenSolver(IonicSolver):                          
      264 +    def solve(self, model, states, dt, Istim):                
      265 +        V = model.get_voltage(states)                         
      266 +        g_inf = model.compute_gate_steady_states(V)           
      267 +        g_tau = model.compute_gate_time_constants(V)          
      268 +        # Gates: m_new = m_inf - (m_inf - m_old) * exp(-dt / t
          +au)                                                           
      269 +        # Voltage: V_new = V + dt * (-Iion + Istim)           
      270 +        # Concentrations: C_new = C + dt * dCdt               
      271 +        return states                                         
      272 +```                                                           
      273 +                                                              
      274 +**`forward_euler.py`** вҖ” Simple Euler for everything (testing/
          +comparison).                                                  
      275 +                                                              
      276 +**`adaptive.py`** вҖ” Variable timestep with error estimation.  
      277 +                                                              
      278 +### `simulation/solvers/diffusion/` вҖ” Diffusion PDE Solvers   
      279 +                                                              
      280 +Each file is one self-contained solver method.                
      281 +                                                              
      282 +**`pcg.py`** вҖ” Pure linear algebra (Ax=b). Knows nothing about
          + physics.                                                     
      283 +                                                              
      284 +**`crank_nicolson.py`** вҖ” 2nd order, unconditionally stable:  
      285 +```python                                                     
      286 +class CrankNicolsonSolver(DiffusionSolver):                   
      287 +    def solve(self, state, dt):                               
      288 +        # Solve: (M + 0.5В·dtВ·K) В· V_new = (M - 0.5В·dtВ·K) В· V_o
          +ld                                                            
      289 +        # Uses PCGSolver internally                           
      290 +```                                                           
      291 +                                                              
      292 +**`bdf1.py`** вҖ” Backward Euler (L-stable, 1st order).         
      293 +                                                              
      294 +**`bdf2.py`** вҖ” BDF2 (A-stable, 2nd order, requires history). 
      295 +                                                              
      296 +### `utils/backend.py` вҖ” Hardware Abstraction                 
      297 +                                                              
      298 +Auto-detects CUDA, MPS (Apple Silicon), or CPU. All tensor cre
          +ation goes through here.                                      
      299 +                                                              
      300 +```python                                                     
      301 +backend = get_backend('auto')  # Returns CUDABackend, MPSBacke
          +nd, or CPUBackend                                             
      302 +x = backend.zeros(100, 100)   # Tensor on correct device      
      303 +backend.sync()                 # Device-appropriate synchroniz
          +ation                                                         
      304 +```                                                           
      305 +                                                              
      306 +---                                                           
      307 +                                                              
      308 +## IonicModel ABC вҖ” Data Provider Interface                   
      309 +                                                              
      310 +```python                                                     
      311 +class IonicModel(ABC):                                        
      312 +    """                                                       
      313 +    Models provide computation FUNCTIONS.                     
      314 +    Models do NOT control stepping order or numerical method. 
      315 +    """                                                       
      316 +                                                              
      317 +    # Identity                                                
      318 +    name: str                                                 
      319 +    n_states: int                                             
      320 +    V_index: int                                              
      321 +    gate_indices: List[int]                                   
      322 +    concentration_indices: List[int]                          
      323 +                                                              
      324 +    # Initialization                                          
      325 +    def get_initial_state(n_cells) -> Tensor: ...             
      326 +                                                              
      327 +    # Computation functions (called by IonicSolver)           
      328 +    def compute_Iion(states) -> Tensor: ...                   
      329 +    def compute_gate_steady_states(V) -> Tensor: ...          
      330 +    def compute_gate_time_constants(V) -> Tensor: ...         
      331 +    def compute_concentration_rates(states) -> Tensor: ...    
      332 +                                                              
      333 +    # Convenience                                             
      334 +    def get_voltage(states) -> Tensor: ...                    
      335 +    def set_voltage(states, V): ...                           
      336 +```                                                           
      337 +                                                              
      338 +---                                                           
      339 +

      356  
      357  ```

      623  
      624  The proposed architecture improves the codebase by:
      625  
      341 -- Grouping mesh with tissue (where it belongs)                
      342 -- Enabling multiple discretization methods (FEM, FDM, FVM)    
      343 -- Separating simulation orchestration from domain logic       
      344 -- Co-locating LUT with the models it accelerates              
      345 -- Preparing for future extensions (bidomain, new ionic models)
      626 +- **Separating physics from numerics** вҖ” ionic models provide 
          +computation functions, solvers decide how to use them         
      627 +- **One file per solver method** вҖ” adding a new solver is addi
          +ng one file, no existing files change                         
      628 +- **Explicit splitting strategies** вҖ” Godunov, Strang, and Sym
          +metric Strang are swappable in `step.py`                      
      629 +- **Absorbed linear solver** вҖ” PCG lives inside `solvers/diffu
          +sion/` where it is used                                       
      630 +- **Grouping mesh with tissue** вҖ” spatial concerns belong toge
          +ther                                                          
      631 +- **Enabling multiple discretization methods** вҖ” FEM, FDM, FVM
          + pluggable                                                    
      632 +- **Co-locating LUT with models** вҖ” lookup tables sit next to 
          +the models they accelerate

          +r NVIDIA vs Apple Silicon

          +on to change

вқҜ i wanted to now scrutinize monodomain/step/and stimulus.py; what contents 
  do we want to put in them                                                 

вҸә Let me trace the data flow through all three files and nail down exactly what
  belongs where.

  The Core Question: Who Owns What?

                      monodomain.py          step.py              stimulus.py
                      в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ          в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ              в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  Owns stimulus?         вң“                                         (is owned)
  Owns step?             вң“                   (is owned)
  Owns state?            вң“
  Owns config?           вң“
  Owns output?           вң“

  Knows about state?     вң“                    вң“
  Knows about model?     вң“ (holds ref)        вң— (receives ref)
  Knows about dt?        вң“ (from config)      вң“ (receives it)
  Knows about time?      вң“ (from state.t)     вң—
  Knows about saving?    вң“                    вң—
  Knows about stimulus?  вң“ (holds ref)        вң“ (receives Istim)    (is it)

  ---
  Decision: Stimulus Ownership

  This is the first boundary to get right.

  OPTION A: step.py owns stimulus              OPTION B: monodomain.py owns
  stimulus
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

  step.py:                                     monodomain.py:
    Istim = self.stimulus.get(state)             Istim =
  self.stimulus.get(state)
    self.ionic.solve(model, states, Istim)       self.stepper.step(state, model,
   dt, Istim)
    self.diffusion.solve(state)
                                               step.py:
                                                 (receives Istim, doesn't know
  source)

  Problem:                                     Advantage:
  Strang calls ionic TWICE,                    step.py is pure numerical
  strategy.
  needs stimulus TWICE.                        stimulus is a simulation concern,
  step.py needs state.t for timing.            not a splitting concern.
  step.py becomes coupled to stimulus.
                                               Problem:
                                               Strang needs Istim twice.
                                               Who calls stimulus the 2nd time?

  Neither option is clean. Here's why:

  STRANG SPLITTING:
    1. ionic(dt/2, Istim_1)      вҶҗ need stimulus at time t
    2. diffusion(dt)
    3. ionic(dt/2, Istim_2)      вҶҗ need stimulus at time t + dt/2 (?)

  The second ionic half-step: should stimulus be re-evaluated?
  - Physically: stimulus is constant over dt (dt = 0.02ms, stimulus lasts 1ms)
  - Practically: same Istim for both halves within one timestep

  So: evaluate stimulus ONCE per timestep, pass it in.

  Decision: monodomain.py evaluates stimulus, passes Istim to step.py.

  ---
  simulation/stimulus.py

  # simulation/stimulus.py
  #
  # RESPONSIBILITIES:
  #   - Define stimulus regions (where to poke)
  #   - Define stimulus timing (when to poke)
  #   - Generate pacing protocols (S1-S2, regular)
  #   - Compute Istim tensor at a given time
  #
  # DOES NOT:
  #   - Know about splitting strategy
  #   - Know about ionic/diffusion solvers
  #   - Manage simulation state (reads state.t, state.nodes)
  #   - Save or output anything


  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
  from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  from typing import List, Callable, Optional, Union
  import torch


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # REGION DEFINITIONS вҖ” "where to poke"
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  class StimulusRegion(ABC):
      """Defines a spatial region for stimulus application."""

      @abstractmethod
      def get_mask(self, nodes: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
          """
          Evaluate region on mesh nodes.
          
          Args:
              nodes: [n_nodes, 2] - x, y coordinates
          Returns:
              mask: [n_nodes] - boolean mask
          """
          ...


  class RectangularRegion(StimulusRegion):
      """Rectangular stimulus region."""

      def __init__(self, x0: float, y0: float, x1: float, y1: float):
          self.x0, self.y0 = x0, y0
          self.x1, self.y1 = x1, y1

      def get_mask(self, nodes):
          x, y = nodes[:, 0], nodes[:, 1]
          return (x >= self.x0) & (x <= self.x1) & (y >= self.y0) & (y <=
  self.y1)


  class CircularRegion(StimulusRegion):
      """Circular stimulus region."""

      def __init__(self, cx: float, cy: float, radius: float):
          self.cx, self.cy, self.radius = cx, cy, radius

      def get_mask(self, nodes):
          dx = nodes[:, 0] - self.cx
          dy = nodes[:, 1] - self.cy
          return (dx * dx + dy * dy) <= self.radius * self.radius


  class EdgeRegion(StimulusRegion):
      """Stimulus along a domain edge."""

      def __init__(self, edge: str = 'left', width: float = 0.1):
          self.edge = edge
          self.width = width

      def get_mask(self, nodes):
          if self.edge == 'left':
              return nodes[:, 0] <= nodes[:, 0].min() + self.width
          elif self.edge == 'right':
              return nodes[:, 0] >= nodes[:, 0].max() - self.width
          elif self.edge == 'bottom':
              return nodes[:, 1] <= nodes[:, 1].min() + self.width
          elif self.edge == 'top':
              return nodes[:, 1] >= nodes[:, 1].max() - self.width


  class CustomRegion(StimulusRegion):
      """Region from arbitrary function."""

      def __init__(self, fn: Callable[[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor], 
  torch.Tensor]):
          self.fn = fn  # fn(x, y) -> bool mask

      def get_mask(self, nodes):
          return self.fn(nodes[:, 0], nodes[:, 1])


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # SINGLE STIMULUS EVENT вҖ” "one poke"
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  @dataclass
  class Stimulus:
      """One stimulus event: region + timing + amplitude."""
      region: StimulusRegion
      start: float              # Start time (ms)
      duration: float           # Duration (ms)
      amplitude: float          # Current amplitude (uA/uF), negative = 
  depolarizing

      @property
      def end(self) -> float:
          return self.start + self.duration


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # STIMULUS PROTOCOL вҖ” "the full pacing plan"
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  class StimulusProtocol:
      """
      Collection of stimulus events with precomputed GPU masks.
      
      Usage:
          protocol = StimulusProtocol()
          protocol.add(EdgeRegion('left', 0.1), start=0, duration=1, 
  amplitude=-52)
          protocol.add_s1s2(...)
          
          protocol.precompute(nodes, device)   # Called once at init
          Istim = protocol.get_current(t)       # Called every timestep
      """

      def __init__(self):
          self.stimuli: List[Stimulus] = []

          # Precomputed GPU tensors (set by precompute())
          self._masks: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None    # [n_stim, n_nodes] bool
          self._starts: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None   # [n_stim] float
          self._ends: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None     # [n_stim] float
          self._amps: Optional[torch.Tensor] = None     # [n_stim] float
          self._n_nodes: int = 0
          self._device = None
          self._precomputed: bool = False

      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Adding stimuli в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

      def add(
          self,
          region: StimulusRegion,
          start: float,
          duration: float,
          amplitude: float
      ):
          """Add a single stimulus event."""
          self.stimuli.append(Stimulus(region, start, duration, amplitude))
          self._precomputed = False  # Invalidate cache

      def add_s1s2(
          self,
          region: StimulusRegion,
          n_s1: int,
          bcl: float,
          s2_ci: float,
          duration: float = 1.0,
          amplitude: float = -52.0,
          s1_start: float = 0.0,
          s2_region: Optional[StimulusRegion] = None,
      ):
          """
          Add S1-S2 pacing protocol.
          
          Args:
              region:     Where to apply S1 stimuli
              n_s1:       Number of S1 beats
              bcl:        Basic cycle length (ms)
              s2_ci:      S2 coupling interval from last S1 (ms)
              duration:   Stimulus duration (ms)
              amplitude:  Stimulus amplitude (uA/uF)
              s1_start:   Time of first S1 (ms)
              s2_region:  Where to apply S2 (defaults to same as S1)
          """
          # S1 beats
          for i in range(n_s1):
              t = s1_start + i * bcl
              self.add(region, t, duration, amplitude)

          # S2 beat
          s2_time = s1_start + (n_s1 - 1) * bcl + s2_ci
          self.add(s2_region or region, s2_time, duration, amplitude)

      def add_regular_pacing(
          self,
          region: StimulusRegion,
          bcl: float,
          n_beats: int,
          start: float = 0.0,
          duration: float = 1.0,
          amplitude: float = -52.0,
      ):
          """Add regular pacing at fixed cycle length."""
          for i in range(n_beats):
              t = start + i * bcl
              self.add(region, t, duration, amplitude)

      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Precomputation в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

      def precompute(self, nodes: torch.Tensor, device: torch.device):
          """
          Precompute all stimulus masks on GPU.
          Called ONCE during simulation initialization.
          
          Args:
              nodes: [n_nodes, 2] - mesh node coordinates (on any device)
              device: Target device for precomputed tensors
          """
          self._device = device
          self._n_nodes = nodes.shape[0]
          n_stim = len(self.stimuli)

          if n_stim == 0:
              self._masks = torch.zeros(0, self._n_nodes, dtype=torch.bool,
  device=device)
              self._starts = torch.zeros(0, device=device)
              self._ends = torch.zeros(0, device=device)
              self._amps = torch.zeros(0, device=device)
              self._precomputed = True
              return

          # Evaluate all regions (may use CPU for lambda functions)
          masks = []
          starts = []
          ends = []
          amps = []

          nodes_cpu = nodes.cpu() if nodes.device != torch.device('cpu') else
  nodes

          for stim in self.stimuli:
              mask = stim.region.get_mask(nodes_cpu)
              masks.append(mask)
              starts.append(stim.start)
              ends.append(stim.end)
              amps.append(stim.amplitude)

          # Stack and move to GPU вҖ” ONE transfer
          self._masks = torch.stack(masks).to(device=device, dtype=torch.bool)
          self._starts = torch.tensor(starts, device=device)
          self._ends = torch.tensor(ends, device=device)
          self._amps = torch.tensor(amps, device=device)
          self._precomputed = True

      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Runtime evaluation в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

      def get_current(self, t: float, Istim: torch.Tensor):
          """
          Compute stimulus current at time t.
          ALL operations on GPU after precompute().
          
          Args:
              t:     Current simulation time (float, from monodomain.py)
              Istim: [n_nodes] pre-allocated output tensor, zeroed by caller
          """
          if not self._precomputed:
              raise RuntimeError("Call precompute() before get_current()")

          if len(self.stimuli) == 0:
              return

          # Which stimuli are active at time t? (GPU comparison)
          active = (t >= self._starts) & (t < self._ends)  # [n_stim] bool

          # Apply active stimuli
          active_indices = torch.where(active)[0]
          for idx in active_indices:
              Istim[self._masks[idx]] = self._amps[idx]

      # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Query в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ

      @property
      def n_stimuli(self) -> int:
          return len(self.stimuli)

      def get_time_range(self) -> tuple:
          """Return (earliest_start, latest_end) across all stimuli."""
          if not self.stimuli:
              return (0.0, 0.0)
          starts = [s.start for s in self.stimuli]
          ends = [s.end for s in self.stimuli]
          return (min(starts), max(ends))

  ---
  simulation/step.py

  # simulation/step.py
  #
  # RESPONSIBILITIES:
  #   - Define splitting strategy (Godunov, Strang, Symmetric Strang)
  #   - Coordinate ionic solver and diffusion solver execution ORDER
  #   - Handle half-step / full-step logic
  #
  # DOES NOT:
  #   - Know about stimulus (receives Istim tensor)
  #   - Know about time tracking (doesn't touch state.t)
  #   - Know about output saving
  #   - Know about config or user API
  #   - Know which specific ionic/diffusion solver is used
  #
  # RECEIVES:
  #   - state: SimulationState (reads/writes state.states, state.pcg_x)
  #   - model: IonicModel reference (passes through to ionic solver)
  #   - dt: timestep (float)
  #   - Istim: stimulus current tensor
  #
  # KEY DESIGN DECISION:
  #   step.py does NOT advance state.t.
  #   monodomain.py advances time after step completes.
  #   This keeps step.py as pure numerical coordination.


  from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
  import torch

  from .solvers.ionic import IonicSolver
  from .solvers.diffusion import DiffusionSolver
  from ..ionic.base import IonicModel
  from .state import SimulationState


  class StepCoordinator(ABC):
      """
      Combines ionic and diffusion solvers into one complete timestep.
      
      This class ONLY decides the ORDER and FRACTION of dt
      given to each solver. It does not:
      - Evaluate stimulus (receives Istim)
      - Track time (doesn't touch state.t)
      - Save output
      """

      def __init__(
          self,
          ionic_solver: IonicSolver,
          diffusion_solver: DiffusionSolver,
      ):
          self.ionic_solver = ionic_solver
          self.diffusion_solver = diffusion_solver

      @abstractmethod
      def step(
          self,
          state: SimulationState,
          model: IonicModel,
          dt: float,
          Istim: torch.Tensor,
      ):
          """
          Execute one complete timestep.
          
          Args:
              state: Simulation state (modified in place)
              model: Ionic model (data provider, not modified)
              dt:    Timestep size (ms)
              Istim: [n_nodes] stimulus current (precomputed by caller)
          
          Postcondition:
              state.states is updated.
              state.t is NOT updated (caller's responsibility).
          """
          ...

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def order(self) -> int:
          """Splitting order: 1 for Godunov, 2 for Strang."""
          ...

      @property
      @abstractmethod
      def name(self) -> str:
          ...


  class GodunovSplitting(StepCoordinator):
      """
      First-order operator splitting.
      
          V^{n+1} = Diffusion(dt) . Ionic(dt) . V^n
      
      Sequence: ionic(dt) вҶ’ diffusion(dt)
      Error: O(dt)
      Cost:  1 ionic + 1 diffusion solve per step
      """

      @property
      def order(self) -> int:
          return 1

      @property
      def name(self) -> str:
          return "Godunov"

      def step(self, state, model, dt, Istim):
          # 1. Full ionic step
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(
              model, state.states, dt, Istim
          )

          # 2. Full diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, dt)


  class StrangSplitting(StepCoordinator):
      """
      Second-order operator splitting (ionic-diffusion-ionic).
      
          V^{n+1} = Ionic(dt/2) . Diffusion(dt) . Ionic(dt/2) . V^n
      
      Sequence: ionic(dt/2) вҶ’ diffusion(dt) вҶ’ ionic(dt/2)
      Error: O(dtВІ)
      Cost:  2 ionic + 1 diffusion solve per step
      
      Best when ionic step is cheaper than diffusion.
      """

      @property
      def order(self) -> int:
          return 2

      @property
      def name(self) -> str:
          return "Strang"

      def step(self, state, model, dt, Istim):
          half = dt / 2.0

          # 1. Half ionic step
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(
              model, state.states, half, Istim
          )

          # 2. Full diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, dt)

          # 3. Half ionic step
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(
              model, state.states, half, Istim
          )


  class SymmetricStrangSplitting(StepCoordinator):
      """
      Second-order operator splitting (diffusion-ionic-diffusion).
      
          V^{n+1} = Diffusion(dt/2) . Ionic(dt) . Diffusion(dt/2) . V^n
      
      Sequence: diffusion(dt/2) вҶ’ ionic(dt) вҶ’ diffusion(dt/2)
      Error: O(dtВІ)
      Cost:  1 ionic + 2 diffusion solves per step
      
      Best when diffusion is the stiffer operator or when
      ionic step is more expensive than diffusion.
      
      Note: Requires diffusion solver to handle variable dt
      (half-step dt differs from cached full-step dt).
      """

      @property
      def order(self) -> int:
          return 2

      @property
      def name(self) -> str:
          return "SymmetricStrang"

      def step(self, state, model, dt, Istim):
          half = dt / 2.0

          # 1. Half diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, half)

          # 2. Full ionic step
          state.states = self.ionic_solver.solve(
              model, state.states, dt, Istim
          )

          # 3. Half diffusion step
          self.diffusion_solver.solve(state, half)

  ---
  simulation/monodomain.py

  # simulation/monodomain.py
  #
  # RESPONSIBILITIES:
  #   - User-facing API (the only file users import)
  #   - Initialize all components from config
  #   - Own state, step coordinator, stimulus, config
  #   - Run simulation loop
  #   - Manage output saving and collection
  #   - Provide analysis utilities (LAT, CV)
  #   - Progress reporting
  #
  # DOES NOT:
  #   - Implement numerical methods (delegates to step.py, solvers/)
  #   - Know about specific solver internals
  #   - Know about specific ionic model internals
  #   - Build FEM matrices (delegates to tissue/discretization/)
  #
  # THIS FILE IS THE GLUE. It wires everything together.


  from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  from typing import Optional, Callable, Tuple, Type
  import torch

  from .state import SimulationState, create_state
  from .step import StepCoordinator, GodunovSplitting, StrangSplitting
  from .stimulus import StimulusProtocol, StimulusRegion
  from .solvers.ionic import IonicSolver
  from .solvers.ionic.rush_larsen import RushLarsenSolver
  from .solvers.diffusion import DiffusionSolver
  from .solvers.diffusion.crank_nicolson import CrankNicolsonSolver
  from .solvers.diffusion.pcg import PCGSolver
  from ..ionic.base import IonicModel
  from ..tissue.mesh import Mesh
  from ..tissue.discretization.base import Discretization
  from ..utils.backend import Backend, get_backend


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # CONFIGURATION
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  @dataclass
  class SimulationConfig:
      """
      All user-configurable simulation parameters.
      Passed to MonodomainSimulation.__init__().
      """
      # Physics
      D: float = 0.001                  # Diffusion coefficient (cmВІ/ms)
      chi: float = 1400.0               # Surface-to-volume ratio (cmвҒ»В№)
      Cm: float = 1.0                   # Membrane capacitance (ВөF/cmВІ)

      # Time
      dt: float = 0.02                  # Timestep (ms)

      # Output
      save_interval: float = 1.0       # Save voltage every N ms
      buffer_size: int = 1000           # Max snapshots before flush

      # Solver selection (swappable)
      ionic_solver: IonicSolver = field(default_factory=RushLarsenSolver)
      diffusion_solver_class: Type[DiffusionSolver] = CrankNicolsonSolver
      splitting_class: Type[StepCoordinator] = GodunovSplitting

      # PCG parameters
      pcg_tol: float = 1e-8
      pcg_max_iter: int = 500
      pcg_check_interval: int = 1       # 1 for Apple, 10+ for NVIDIA

      # Device
      device: str = 'auto'              # 'auto', 'cuda', 'mps', 'cpu'


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # MAIN SIMULATION CLASS
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  class MonodomainSimulation:
      """
      Top-level simulation API.
      
      This is the only class users need to interact with.
      All internal components are assembled here from config.
      
      Usage:
          sim = MonodomainSimulation(mesh, model, config)
          sim.add_stimulus(EdgeRegion('left'), start=0, duration=1, 
  amplitude=-52)
          times, voltages = sim.run(t_end=500.0)
      """

      def __init__(
          self,
          mesh: Mesh,
          ionic_model: IonicModel,
          config: SimulationConfig = SimulationConfig(),
      ):
          self.config = config
          self.ionic_model = ionic_model

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Backend в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self.backend = get_backend(config.device)

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Discretization & matrices в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self._discretization = self._build_discretization(mesh, config)
          M, K = self._discretization.assemble(mesh, config.D, config.chi,
  config.Cm)

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ State в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self.state = create_state(
              mesh=mesh,
              ionic_model=ionic_model,
              M=M,
              K=K,
              config=config,
              device=self.backend.device,
          )

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Stimulus в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self.stimulus = StimulusProtocol()

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Solvers в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          pcg = PCGSolver(
              n=mesh.n_nodes,
              device=self.backend.device,
              tol=config.pcg_tol,
              max_iter=config.pcg_max_iter,
              check_interval=config.pcg_check_interval,
          )

          diffusion_solver = config.diffusion_solver_class(
              M=M,
              K=K,
              pcg=pcg,
          )

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Step coordinator в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self.stepper = config.splitting_class(
              ionic_solver=config.ionic_solver,
              diffusion_solver=diffusion_solver,
          )

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Output tracking в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self._save_counter: float = 0.0
          self._output_times: list = []

          # в”Җв”Җв”Җ Pre-allocated stimulus tensor в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
          self._Istim = torch.zeros(
              mesh.n_nodes, device=self.backend.device, dtype=self.backend.dtype
          )

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # STIMULUS API
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def add_stimulus(
          self,
          region: StimulusRegion,
          start: float,
          duration: float,
          amplitude: float,
      ):
          """Add a single stimulus event."""
          self.stimulus.add(region, start, duration, amplitude)

      def add_s1s2(self, region, n_s1, bcl, s2_ci, **kwargs):
          """Add S1-S2 pacing protocol."""
          self.stimulus.add_s1s2(region, n_s1, bcl, s2_ci, **kwargs)

      def add_regular_pacing(self, region, bcl, n_beats, **kwargs):
          """Add regular pacing protocol."""
          self.stimulus.add_regular_pacing(region, bcl, n_beats, **kwargs)

      def _finalize_stimulus(self):
          """Precompute stimulus masks. Called once before first step."""
          if not self.stimulus._precomputed:
              self.stimulus.precompute(self.state.nodes, self.backend.device)

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # SIMULATION EXECUTION
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def step(self):
          """
          Execute ONE complete timestep.
          
          Sequence:
          1. Evaluate stimulus at current time
          2. Delegate to step coordinator (ionic + diffusion)
          3. Advance time
          4. Save output if at save interval
          """
          dt = self.config.dt

          # 1. Get stimulus current
          self._Istim.zero_()
          t_current = self.state.t.item()
          self.stimulus.get_current(t_current, self._Istim)

          # 2. Step (ionic + diffusion in configured order)
          self.stepper.step(self.state, self.ionic_model, dt, self._Istim)

          # 3. Advance time
          self.state.t = self.state.t + dt

          # 4. Save if at interval
          self._maybe_save_output(dt)

      def run(
          self,
          t_end: float,
          progress_callback: Optional[Callable[[float, float], None]] = None,
          progress_interval: int = 1000,
      ) -> Tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
          """
          Run simulation from current time to t_end.
          
          Args:
              t_end:             End time (ms)
              progress_callback: fn(current_time, t_end) called periodically
              progress_interval: Steps between progress reports
          
          Returns:
              times:    [n_saves] - saved time points (ms)
              voltages: [n_saves, n_nodes] - saved voltage snapshots
          """
          # Finalize stimulus (precompute masks)
          self._finalize_stimulus()

          n_steps = int(t_end / self.config.dt)

          for i in range(n_steps):
              self.step()

              if progress_callback and (i + 1) % progress_interval == 0:
                  t_now = self.state.t.item()
                  progress_callback(t_now, t_end)

          return self._collect_outputs()

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # OUTPUT MANAGEMENT
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def _maybe_save_output(self, dt: float):
          """Save voltage snapshot if at save interval."""
          self._save_counter += dt

          if self._save_counter >= self.config.save_interval - 1e-10:
              self._save_counter = 0.0

              V = self.state.states[:, self.ionic_model.V_index]

              idx = self.state.buffer_idx
              if idx < self.config.buffer_size:
                  self.state.output_buffer[idx] = V
                  self.state.buffer_idx += 1
                  self._output_times.append(self.state.t.item())

      def _collect_outputs(self) -> Tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
          """Collect saved outputs from GPU buffer."""
          idx = self.state.buffer_idx

          if idx == 0:
              n = self.state.n_nodes
              return torch.zeros(0), torch.zeros(0, n)

          voltages = self.state.output_buffer[:idx]  # Still on device
          times = torch.tensor(self._output_times)

          return times, voltages

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # ANALYSIS UTILITIES
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def compute_activation_time(
          self,
          voltages: torch.Tensor,
          times: torch.Tensor,
          threshold: float = -20.0,
      ) -> torch.Tensor:
          """
          Compute local activation time (LAT) at each node.
          
          Args:
              voltages:  [n_times, n_nodes] from run()
              times:     [n_times] from run()
              threshold: Voltage threshold for activation (mV)
          
          Returns:
              lat: [n_nodes] activation time at each node (ms)
          """
          above = voltages > threshold          # [n_times, n_nodes] bool
          first = above.float().argmax(dim=0)   # [n_nodes] first index above 
  threshold
          return times[first]

      def compute_conduction_velocity(
          self,
          voltages: torch.Tensor,
          times: torch.Tensor,
          p1: Tuple[float, float],
          p2: Tuple[float, float],
          threshold: float = -20.0,
      ) -> float:
          """
          Compute conduction velocity between two points.
          
          Args:
              voltages, times: from run()
              p1, p2: (x, y) coordinates of measurement points
              threshold: activation threshold (mV)
          
          Returns:
              CV in cm/s
          """
          lat = self.compute_activation_time(voltages, times, threshold)

          nodes = self.state.nodes
          d1 = ((nodes[:, 0] - p1[0])**2 + (nodes[:, 1] - p1[1])**2)
          d2 = ((nodes[:, 0] - p2[0])**2 + (nodes[:, 1] - p2[1])**2)

          idx1 = d1.argmin()
          idx2 = d2.argmin()

          dt_activation = (lat[idx2] - lat[idx1]).item()  # ms
          distance = torch.sqrt(
              (nodes[idx2, 0] - nodes[idx1, 0])**2 +
              (nodes[idx2, 1] - nodes[idx1, 1])**2
          ).item()  # cm

          if abs(dt_activation) < 1e-10:
              return float('inf')

          return (distance / dt_activation) * 1000  # cm/s (convert ms to s)

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # STATE ACCESS
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def get_voltage(self) -> torch.Tensor:
          """Get current voltage field. Returns [n_nodes] tensor on device."""
          return self.state.states[:, self.ionic_model.V_index]

      def get_time(self) -> float:
          """Get current simulation time in ms."""
          return self.state.t.item()

      @property
      def info(self) -> str:
          """Summary of simulation configuration."""
          return (
              f"MonodomainSimulation:\n"
              f"  Nodes:      {self.state.n_nodes}\n"
              f"  States:     {self.state.n_states} ({self.ionic_model.name})\n"
              f"  dt:         {self.config.dt} ms\n"
              f"  Splitting:  {self.stepper.name} (order 
  {self.stepper.order})\n"
              f"  Ionic:      {type(self.config.ionic_solver).__name__}\n"
              f"  Diffusion:  {self.config.diffusion_solver_class.__name__}\n"
              f"  Device:     {self.backend.device}\n"
              f"  Stimuli:    {self.stimulus.n_stimuli}\n"
          )

      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
      # INTERNAL HELPERS
      # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

      def _build_discretization(self, mesh, config):
          """Build discretization from mesh type. Override for custom."""
          from ..tissue.discretization.fem import FEMDiscretization
          return FEMDiscretization()

  вҺҝ В Interrupted В· What should Claude do instead?

вқҜ i would recommend renameing step into solver; breaking down into a main   
  solver.py, then couple of strategy files. it owns stimulus and is called

вҸә Mixed. The naming and structure changes are good. Stimulus ownership is
  debatable. Here's the breakdown:

  Renaming step вҶ’ solver + Strategy Files: Good

  CURRENT:                              PROPOSED:
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                              в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  simulation/                           simulation/
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ step.py  (3 classes in 1 file)    в”ңв”Җв”Җ solver/
  в”Ӯ                                     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ __init__.py         #
  MonodomainSolver
  в”Ӯ                                     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ godunov.py          #
  GodunovSplitting
  в”Ӯ                                     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ strang.py           #
  StrangSplitting
  в”Ӯ                                     в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ symmetric_strang.py
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ solvers/                          в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/                        в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ rush_larsen.py
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ rush_larsen.py            в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ forward_euler.py
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ...                       в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adaptive.py
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ diffusion/                    в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ diffusion/
  в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ pcg.py                    в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ pcg.py
  в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ ...                       в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ crank_nicolson.py
  в”Ӯ                                     в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ bdf1.py
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ monodomain.py                     в”ңв”Җв”Җ monodomain.py
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ state.py                          в”ңв”Җв”Җ state.py
  в””в”Җв”Җ stimulus.py                       в””в”Җв”Җ stimulus.py

  This is an improvement because:
  - "solver" is more accurate than "step"
  - One strategy per file (consistent with one-file-per-method principle)
  - All solving logic under one folder hierarchy

  ---
  Stimulus Ownership: Tradeoff

  Option A: Solver Owns Stimulus (your proposal)

  # monodomain.py вҖ” thin, clean
  class MonodomainSimulation:
      def step(self):
          self.solver.step(self.state, self.ionic_model, self.config.dt)
          self.state.t += self.config.dt
          self._maybe_save()

  # solver/__init__.py вҖ” owns stimulus
  class MonodomainSolver:
      def __init__(self, strategy, ionic, diffusion, stimulus):
          self.strategy = strategy
          self.ionic = ionic
          self.diffusion = diffusion
          self.stimulus = stimulus       # вҶҗ solver owns it

      def step(self, state, model, dt):
          Istim = self._get_stimulus(state.t)
          self.strategy.execute(state, model, dt, Istim, self.ionic,
  self.diffusion)

  Pros:                                    Cons:
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                    в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  вң“ monodomain.step() is one line          вң— Solver knows about time (state.t)
  вң“ No Istim plumbing in monodomain        вң— Stimulus is physics, not numerics
  вң“ Solver is self-contained unit          вң— Strategy files still receive Istim
  вң“ Cleaner call interface                 вң— Users add stimuli through solver
                                           вң— Swapping solver requires moving
  stimulus

  Option B: Monodomain Owns Stimulus (current design)

  # monodomain.py вҖ” owns stimulus
  class MonodomainSimulation:
      def step(self):
          self._Istim.zero_()
          self.stimulus.get_current(self.state.t, self._Istim)
          self.solver.step(self.state, self.ionic_model, self.config.dt,
  self._Istim)
          self.state.t += self.config.dt
          self._maybe_save()

  # solver/__init__.py вҖ” receives Istim
  class MonodomainSolver:
      def step(self, state, model, dt, Istim):
          self.strategy.execute(state, model, dt, Istim, self.ionic,
  self.diffusion)

  Pros:                                    Cons:
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                                    в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  вң“ Solver is pure numerics               вң— monodomain.step() has Istim plumbing
  вң“ Stimulus is simulation concern         вң— Extra parameter passing
  вң“ Swap solver without touching stimulus
  вң“ Strategy files never know stimulus

  ---
  Honest Assessment

  Option A is the better design if we accept one thing: the solver is not just
  "numerics" вҖ” it's the complete timestep unit, which includes stimulus as an
  input.

  The question is what "solver" means:

  NARROW definition (pure math):        BROAD definition (complete step):
  Solver = ionic + diffusion + split     Solver = stimulus + ionic + diffusion +
   split

  Stimulus is external input.            Stimulus is part of the step.
  monodomain passes it in.               Solver handles it internally.

  Your proposal uses the broad definition. That's defensible because:

  stimulus вҶ’ ionic вҶ’ diffusion
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  All three happen inside ONE timestep.
  The solver is "everything that happens in one dt."
  monodomain is "everything that happens across many dt."

  ---
  Recommendation: Accept With One Constraint

  Accept your proposal, but keep the strategy files unaware of stimulus.
  Stimulus lives in the solver wrapper, not the strategy:

  simulation/
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ monodomain.py              # Loop, output, user API
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ state.py                   # Data container
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ stimulus.py                # StimulusProtocol (unchanged)
  в”Ӯ
  в””в”Җв”Җ solver/
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ __init__.py            # MonodomainSolver (owns stimulus, dispatches)
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ base.py                # SplittingStrategy ABC
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ godunov.py             # GodunovSplitting (receives Istim)
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ strang.py              # StrangSplitting (receives Istim)
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ symmetric_strang.py    # SymmetricStrangSplitting (receives Istim)
      в”Ӯ
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic/
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ __init__.py        # IonicSolver ABC
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ rush_larsen.py
      в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ forward_euler.py
      в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ adaptive.py
      в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җ diffusion/
          в”ңв”Җв”Җ __init__.py        # DiffusionSolver ABC
          в”ңв”Җв”Җ pcg.py
          в”ңв”Җв”Җ crank_nicolson.py
          в”ңв”Җв”Җ bdf1.py
          в””в”Җв”Җ bdf2.py

  How it works:

  # solver/__init__.py вҖ” the wrapper
  class MonodomainSolver:
      """
      Complete timestep solver.
      Owns stimulus. Dispatches to splitting strategy.
      Strategy files never see stimulus.
      """

      def __init__(self, strategy, ionic, diffusion, stimulus, n_nodes, device):
          self.strategy = strategy       # GodunovSplitting, etc.
          self.ionic = ionic             # RushLarsenSolver, etc.
          self.diffusion = diffusion     # CrankNicolsonSolver, etc.
          self.stimulus = stimulus       # StimulusProtocol
          self._Istim = torch.zeros(n_nodes, device=device)

      def step(self, state, model, dt):
          """One complete timestep. Called by monodomain."""
          # Stimulus evaluation (solver's job)
          self._Istim.zero_()
          self.stimulus.get_current(state.t, self._Istim)

          # Dispatch to strategy (strategy doesn't know about stimulus)
          self.strategy.execute(
              state, model, dt, self._Istim,
              self.ionic, self.diffusion
          )


  # solver/godunov.py вҖ” pure numerical strategy
  class GodunovSplitting(SplittingStrategy):
      """Receives Istim. Doesn't know where it came from."""

      def execute(self, state, model, dt, Istim, ionic, diffusion):
          state.states = ionic.solve(model, state.states, dt, Istim)
          diffusion.solve(state, dt)


  # solver/strang.py вҖ” pure numerical strategy
  class StrangSplitting(SplittingStrategy):

      def execute(self, state, model, dt, Istim, ionic, diffusion):
          half = dt / 2.0
          state.states = ionic.solve(model, state.states, half, Istim)
          diffusion.solve(state, dt)
          state.states = ionic.solve(model, state.states, half, Istim)


  # monodomain.py вҖ” thin
  class MonodomainSimulation:

      def step(self):
          self.solver.step(self.state, self.ionic_model, self.config.dt)
          self.state.t += self.config.dt
          self._maybe_save()

      # Stimulus API passes through to solver
      def add_stimulus(self, region, start, duration, amplitude):
          self.solver.stimulus.add(region, start, duration, amplitude)

  Call chain:

  monodomain.step()
      в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв–ә solver.step(state, model, dt)          solver/__init__.py
              в”Ӯ
              в”ңв”Җв”Җ stimulus.get_current(t, Istim)   stimulus.py
              в”Ӯ
              в””в”Җв”Җ strategy.execute(..., Istim)      solver/godunov.py
                      в”Ӯ
                      в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic.solve()              solver/ionic/rush_larsen.py
                      в””в”Җв”Җ diffusion.solve()
  solver/diffusion/crank_nicolson.py

  Updated responsibility:

  FILE                      OWNS                KNOWS ABOUT
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ    в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  monodomain.py             state, config        solver (as black box)
                            output, loop         time advancement

  solver/__init__.py        stimulus             state.t (for stimulus eval)
                            strategy ref         ionic, diffusion, strategy
                            Istim tensor

  solver/godunov.py         nothing              ionic, diffusion (as args)
  solver/strang.py          nothing              ionic, diffusion (as args)

  solver/ionic/*            nothing              model compute functions
  solver/diffusion/*        nothing              matrices, PCG

  stimulus.py               masks, timing        node coordinates (at init)

  Strategy files stay pure math. Stimulus coupling is isolated in the solver
  wrapper. Monodomain is thin. Want me to update improvement.md with this?

      288 +### `simulation/solver/splitting/` вҖ” Splitting Strategies     
      289 +                                                              
      290 +Each file is one strategy. Receives Istim вҖ” doesn't know where
          + it came from.                                                
      291 +                                                              
      292 +**`splitting/__init__.py`** вҖ” The ABC:                        
      293 +```python                                                     
      294 +class SplittingStrategy(ABC):                                 
      295 +    @abstractmethod                                           
      296 +    def execute(self, state, model, dt, Istim, ionic, diffusio
          +n): ...                                                       
      297 +                                                              
      298 +    @property                                                 
      299 +    @abstractmethod                                           
      300 +    def order(self) -> int: ...                               
      301 +                                                              
      302 +    @property                                                 
      303 +    @abstractmethod                                           
      304 +    def name(self) -> str: ...                                
      305 +```                                                           
      306 +                                                              
      307 +**`splitting/godunov.py`** вҖ” 1st order:                       
      308 +```python                                                     
      309 +class GodunovSplitting(SplittingStrategy):                    
      310 +    """ionic(dt) вҶ’ diffusion(dt). Error O(dt)."""             
      311 +    order = 1                                                 
      312 +    name = "Godunov"                                          
      313 +                                                              
      314 +    def execute(self, state, model, dt, Istim, ionic, diffusio
          +n):                                                           
      315 +        state.states = ionic.solve(model, state.states, dt, Is
          +tim)                                                          
      316 +        diffusion.solve(state, dt)                            
      317 +```                                                           
      318 +

      621  | **Discretization** | FEM only | FEM/FDM/FVM pluggable | Exte
           nsible to new methods |
      622  | **LUT location** | `ionic/lut.py` | `ionic/models/lut.py` | 
           Co-located with models it serves |
      623  | **Simulation** | Inside `tissue/` | Top-level `simulation/` 
           | Clear entry point |
      500 -| **step() location** | Inside each ionic model | `simulation/
          -solvers/ionic/` | Physics separated from numerics |           
      501 -| **Solver location** | Top-level `solver/` | `simulation/solv
          -ers/diffusion/` | Grouped with what it serves |               
      502 -| **Splitting strategy** | Hardcoded Godunov | Swappable via `
          -step.py` | Godunov/Strang/Symmetric |                         
      624 +| **step() location** | Inside each ionic model | `solver/ioni
          +c/` | Physics separated from numerics |                       
      625 +| **Linear solver** | Top-level `solver/` | `solver/diffusion/
          +pcg.py` | Grouped with what it serves |                       
      626 +| **Splitting strategy** | Hardcoded Godunov | `solver/splitti
          +ng/{method}.py` | Swappable, one file each |                  
      627 +| **Stimulus ownership** | `tissue/stimulus.py` | Solver owns,
          + `stimulus.py` defines | Part of timestep unit |              
      628  | **Adding a solver** | Edit existing files | Add one new file
            | Open-closed principle |
      629  | **Ionic model role** | Physics + stepping | Physics only (da
           ta provider) | Single responsibility |

      792  The proposed architecture improves the codebase by:
      793  
      794  - **Separating physics from numerics** вҖ” ionic models provide 
           computation functions, solvers decide how to use them
      627 -- **One file per solver method** вҖ” adding a new solver is addi
          -ng one file, no existing files change                         
      628 -- **Explicit splitting strategies** вҖ” Godunov, Strang, and Sym
          -metric Strang are swappable in `step.py`                      
      629 -- **Absorbed linear solver** вҖ” PCG lives inside `solvers/diffu
          -sion/` where it is used                                       
      795 +- **One file per method** вҖ” adding a new solver or splitting s
          +trategy is adding one file, no existing files change          
      796 +- **Solver as complete timestep unit** вҖ” `solver/` owns stimul
          +us, splitting, ionic, and diffusion                           
      797 +- **Three parallel solver concerns** вҖ” `splitting/`, `ionic/`,
          + `diffusion/` each handle one concept                         
      798 +- **Strategy files stay pure** вҖ” splitting strategies receive 
          +Istim, don't know about stimulus                              
      799 +- **Thin monodomain.py** вҖ” only loop, save, progress, and user
          + API                                                          
      800  - **Grouping mesh with tissue** вҖ” spatial concerns belong toge
           ther
      801  - **Enabling multiple discretization methods** вҖ” FEM, FDM, FVM
            pluggable
      802  - **Co-locating LUT with models** вҖ” lookup tables sit next to 
           the models they accelerate

вҸә improvement.md updated with the final architecture:

  - solver/ now contains three parallel subfolders: splitting/, ionic/,
  diffusion/
  - solver/__init__.py (MonodomainSolver) owns stimulus and dispatches to
  splitting strategy
  - Splitting strategies in their own folder with one file per method
  - All diagrams, flow charts, responsibility matrices, and data flow updated to
   reflect the new structure
  - Import paths updated (e.g., simulation.solver.splitting.strang)
