вқҜ /export 
  вҺҝ  Conversation exported to:
     2026-01-28-read-over-all-stuff-in-monodomain-v53.txt

вқҜ walk though an example of implementing a s1-s2 protocal in a anisotrpic   
  tissue; from the implementation pof                                       
  вҺҝ В Interrupted В· What should Claude do instead?

вқҜ according to our current structure; did we make compartmentalization easy 
  enough for different backend implementation strategy to happen?           

вҸә Short answer: partially. Backend handles device-level operations, but
  platform-specific strategies that span multiple components aren't cleanly
  compartmentalized yet.

  Where It Works

  utils/backend.py handles:
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  вң“ Tensor creation (zeros, ones, tensor)
  вң“ Device selection (cuda, mps, cpu)
  вң“ Synchronization (cuda.sync vs mps.sync vs pass)
  вң“ Cache management (empty_cache)
  вң“ dtype selection (float64 for CUDA, float32 for MPS)

  These are low-level operations. One interface, three implementations. Clean.

  Where It Falls Apart

  Platform differences go deeper than tensor creation. They affect strategy 
  choices across multiple files:

                            NVIDIA              APPLE SILICON          CPU
                            в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ              в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ          в•җв•җв•җ
  PCG convergence check     Fixed iters         Every 5 iters         Every iter
  (solver/diffusion/pcg)    (no .item())        (.item() cheap)       (no cost)

  Stimulus evaluation       Precomputed masks   Can be lazy            Can be
  lazy
  (solver/__init__)         (no CPUвҶ’GPU)        (unified memory)       (no
  transfer)

  Output saving             GPU ring buffer     Direct clone           Direct
  save
  (monodomain.py)           batch at end        (unified memory)       (no
  transfer)

  Ionic kernel strategy     @torch.compile      Standard PyTorch       NumPy
  possible
  (solver/ionic/*)          fused kernels       (MPS compile limited)  (no GPU)

  These differences span four separate files. Right now we handle them with
  config parameters:

  config = SimulationConfig(
      pcg_check_interval=50,     # вҶҗ NVIDIA user must know to set this
      buffer_size=1000,          # вҶҗ NVIDIA user must know to set this
      # ... user has to understand platform tradeoffs
  )

  Problem: The user shouldn't need to know PCG convergence check frequency
  depends on their GPU vendor.

  The Gap

  CURRENT ARCHITECTURE:

      backend.py                          solver/, monodomain.py
      в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ                          в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
      "What device am I on?"              "What strategy should I use?"
                в”Ӯ                                    в”Ӯ
                в”Ӯ                                    в”Ӯ
                в–ј                                    в–ј
      Device-level abstraction            Config parameters (manual)

      These two don't talk to each other.
      Backend doesn't inform solver strategy.

  Solution: Platform Profile

  Add one layer that bridges backend вҶ’ solver strategy. Not per-file variants вҖ”
  a single profile that configures everything.

  cardiac_sim/
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ utils/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ backend.py                    # Device abstraction (unchanged)
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ platform.py                   # NEW: Platform optimization profile
  в”Ӯ
  в”ңв”Җв”Җ simulation/
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ solver/
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ diffusion/
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ pcg.py               # Uses profile.pcg_check_interval
  в”Ӯ   в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ...
  в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ monodomain.py                 # Uses profile.output_strategy
  в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ...

  utils/platform.py

  # utils/platform.py
  #
  # Bridges backend (what hardware) вҶ’ solver strategy (how to optimize).
  # ONE file that captures ALL platform-specific decisions.

  from dataclasses import dataclass
  from enum import Enum
  import torch


  class OutputStrategy(Enum):
      GPU_BUFFER = "gpu_buffer"       # Accumulate on GPU, bulk transfer
      DIRECT_CLONE = "direct_clone"   # Clone per save (unified memory)
      DIRECT_SAVE = "direct_save"     # No transfer needed (CPU)


  class StimulusStrategy(Enum):
      PRECOMPUTED = "precomputed"     # All masks on GPU at init
      LAZY = "lazy"                   # Evaluate per step (cheap transfers)


  @dataclass(frozen=True)
  class PlatformProfile:
      """
      All platform-specific optimization decisions in one place.
      
      Generated automatically from detected hardware.
      User can override any field.
      """
      # PCG solver
      pcg_check_interval: int         # How often to check convergence
      pcg_fixed_iters: bool           # Use fixed iteration count?
      pcg_default_iters: int          # Default iteration count if fixed

      # Output
      output_strategy: OutputStrategy
      output_buffer_size: int         # Ring buffer size (if GPU_BUFFER)

      # Stimulus
      stimulus_strategy: StimulusStrategy

      # Ionic solver
      use_torch_compile: bool         # Fuse kernels with @torch.compile

      # Precision
      default_dtype: torch.dtype

      # Sync behavior
      sync_cost: str                  # "high" (NVIDIA), "low" (Apple), "none" 
  (CPU)


  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ
  # PRE-BUILT PROFILES
  # в•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җв•җ

  CUDA_PROFILE = PlatformProfile(
      pcg_check_interval=50,
      pcg_fixed_iters=True,
      pcg_default_iters=50,
      output_strategy=OutputStrategy.GPU_BUFFER,
      output_buffer_size=1000,
      stimulus_strategy=StimulusStrategy.PRECOMPUTED,
      use_torch_compile=True,
      default_dtype=torch.float64,
      sync_cost="high",
  )

  MPS_PROFILE = PlatformProfile(
      pcg_check_interval=5,
      pcg_fixed_iters=False,
      pcg_default_iters=200,
      output_strategy=OutputStrategy.DIRECT_CLONE,
      output_buffer_size=0,
      stimulus_strategy=StimulusStrategy.PRECOMPUTED,  # Still good practice
      use_torch_compile=False,                          # MPS compile limited
      default_dtype=torch.float32,                      # MPS prefers float32
      sync_cost="low",
  )

  CPU_PROFILE = PlatformProfile(
      pcg_check_interval=1,
      pcg_fixed_iters=False,
      pcg_default_iters=500,
      output_strategy=OutputStrategy.DIRECT_SAVE,
      output_buffer_size=0,
      stimulus_strategy=StimulusStrategy.LAZY,
      use_torch_compile=False,
      default_dtype=torch.float64,
      sync_cost="none",
  )


  def get_platform_profile(device: str = 'auto') -> PlatformProfile:
      """Auto-detect platform and return optimized profile."""
      if device == 'auto':
          if torch.cuda.is_available():
              return CUDA_PROFILE
          elif torch.backends.mps.is_available():
              return MPS_PROFILE
          else:
              return CPU_PROFILE
      elif device == 'cuda':
          return CUDA_PROFILE
      elif device == 'mps':
          return MPS_PROFILE
      else:
          return CPU_PROFILE

  How It Flows Through the Architecture

  User creates simulation
      в”Ӯ
      в–ј
  MonodomainSimulation.__init__()
      в”Ӯ
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ backend = get_backend('auto')           # utils/backend.py
      в”ңв”Җв”Җ profile = get_platform_profile('auto')  # utils/platform.py
      в”Ӯ
      в”Ӯ   Profile flows into each component:
      в”Ӯ
      в”ңв”Җв”Җв–ә PCGSolver(check_interval=profile.pcg_check_interval)
      в”Ӯ                                           # solver/diffusion/pcg.py
      в”Ӯ
      в”ңв”Җв”Җв–ә MonodomainSolver(stimulus_strategy=profile.stimulus_strategy)
      в”Ӯ                                           # solver/__init__.py
      в”Ӯ
      в”ңв”Җв”Җв–ә output_strategy=profile.output_strategy
      в”Ӯ                                           # monodomain.py save logic
      в”Ӯ
      в””в”Җв”Җв–ә IonicSolver(use_compile=profile.use_torch_compile)
                                                  # solver/ionic/rush_larsen.py

  BEFORE: User sets platform params manually
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  config = SimulationConfig(
      pcg_check_interval=50,      # "Why 50?"
      buffer_size=1000,            # "Why 1000?"
      use_torch_compile=True,      # "Should I?"
  )

  AFTER: Auto-detected, user can override
  в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ
  config = SimulationConfig(
      dt=0.02,                     # User only sets physics params
      D=0.001,
  )
  # Platform optimization happens automatically.

  # Or override one thing:
  config = SimulationConfig(
      platform_overrides={'pcg_check_interval': 10}
  )

  Updated Architecture
